
-----title
峡江（新淦） (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='46a22d5c3da747fdbd94cd39c9868a6d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("46a22d5c3da747fdbd94cd39c9868a6d");'><span id='46a22d5c3da747fdbd94cd39c9868a6d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1062')">1042-1062年</a>，1-21岁</div><div id='46a22d5c3da747fdbd94cd39c9868a6d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年7月15日</a>　居乡。武仲生，父延之登进士榜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年6月9日</a>　居乡。六月九日，弟孔平仲生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　居乡。父延之作《宋桂州瘗宜贼首级记》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1055')">1046-1055年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　居乡。兄文仲应乡举。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　居乡。兄文仲再应乡举。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　居乡。应乡举。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　居乡。兄文仲登进士第，调余杭尉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　居乡。武仲为国子解魁。弟平仲中乡举。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
开封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3ae5c088439d43309cf39d265b587aaf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3ae5c088439d43309cf39d265b587aaf");'><span id='3ae5c088439d43309cf39d265b587aaf_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>，22岁</div><div id='3ae5c088439d43309cf39d265b587aaf' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>　登进士第，授穀城主簿。作品：谢及第启。<div id='poem_1194028' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194028' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194028?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢及第启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194028")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194028_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194028'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194028'>法座颙昂，广览四方之俊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194028_comment'></div>儒冠杂沓，同升一命之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194028_comment'></div>顾惟庸鄙之资，亦预优殊之等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194028_comment'></div>逢辰幸甚，揣己自惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194028_comment'></div>独以为国者得士而昌，济世者取人尤急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194028_comment'></div>宾贤能以三物，粤自乎成周之隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194028_comment'></div>求儒阐乎大猷，益盛于西汉之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194028_comment'></div>自是以降，为法不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194028_comment'></div>或收孝廉，或举茂异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194028_comment'></div>尚经术者，或起辨争之论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194028_comment'></div>取时文者，或被浮华之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194028_comment'></div>然而豪俊亦出于其间，国家常赖以为助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194028_comment'></div>揭为成宪，贻厥来今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194028_comment'></div>本朝绍三代之太平，讲百王之遗美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194028_comment'></div>重围沓矩，粹礼乐以陶斯民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194028_comment'></div>流风馀波，一华夷以变于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194028_comment'></div>家习俎豆，里有弦歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194028_comment'></div>薰蒸醇酿，振发光景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194028_comment'></div>矧乎京师首善，远追四学之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194028_comment'></div>有司校文，增用间年之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194028_comment'></div>法度皦乎昼日，请托绝于秋毫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194028_comment'></div>穷山取材，梗楠归匠氏之巧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1194028_comment'></div>极深宠宝，珠贝登庙器之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1194028_comment'></div>飘风泛乎卷阿，众流归于巨海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1194028_comment'></div>罕遗于野，争立于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1194028_comment'></div>晏然极治之时，皇矣多士之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1194028_comment'></div>自非尤异，难冒宠灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1194028_comment'></div>如某者，抱斗筲之小才，承箕裘之素业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1194028_comment'></div>少而好戏，时人皆笑其愚顽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1194028_comment'></div>长匪通方，诗律仅分于竞病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1194028_comment'></div>而自再被斥于乡举，一偕计于使台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1194028_comment'></div>念终军弃繻之年，宜观于上国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1194028_comment'></div>服扬子求师之戒，遂齿于诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1194028_comment'></div>惜寸阴以竞辰，张短檠而继日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1194028_comment'></div>杜门几于不出，取友期于必端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1194028_comment'></div>作赋虽勤，未窥虫篆之巧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1194028_comment'></div>读书务博，不免涉猎之粗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1194028_comment'></div>顾末学之何堪，辱诸公之与进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1194028_comment'></div>桥门试艺，偶窃冠于朋来；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1194028_comment'></div>宗伯程能，复当举于首选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1194028_comment'></div>指拙为巧，颇闻众议之欢哗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1194028_comment'></div>以浅测深，适会天题之闳奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1194028_comment'></div>重以九阍列戟，百辟在廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1194028_comment'></div>密迩威显，顾瞻驶景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1194028_comment'></div>干魂欲落，窃惊帝所之游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1194028_comment'></div>利害未忘，更怀金注之感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1194028_comment'></div>吟吻几噪，抽思愈穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1194028_comment'></div>聊因笔墨之成文，难与麒麟而争路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1194028_comment'></div>退惟疏略，默俟报闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1194028_comment'></div>及便殿之胪传，方堵墙而竦听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1194028_comment'></div>偶叨前列，实越初心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1194028_comment'></div>加以自幽迁乔，不牵于常格；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1194028_comment'></div>提衡引重，又出于大臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1194028_comment'></div>泽滂草莱，悸发梦寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1194028_comment'></div>非能自致，实有所缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1194028_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官以夔龙之贤，佐佑明上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1194028_comment'></div>以周孔之道，启迪当时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1194028_comment'></div>育养英才，爰若中陵之甚厚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1194028_comment'></div>采收小善，不以下体而见遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1194028_comment'></div>能者引类而皆来，否者闻风而胥劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1194028_comment'></div>分庭抗礼，几忘于尊卑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1194028_comment'></div>开閤见贤，不私于远近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1194028_comment'></div>风流之及，罢懦以兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1194028_comment'></div>遂令闾巷之小生，亦分升斗之微禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1194028_comment'></div>敢不益求师范，每励官箴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1194028_comment'></div>佩圣训于中庸，止思言行之相顾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1194028_comment'></div>诵诗声于大雅，更期明哲以保身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1194028_comment'></div>披之以抱关击柝，而敢不固穷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1194028_comment'></div>用之于班朝治军，而或将有立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1194028_comment'></div>庶成薄效，以报大恩。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_69_1194028'></div><div id='poem_sentence_69_1194028_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='aa1f4f6a8aa54ff58481867d712b154d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("aa1f4f6a8aa54ff58481867d712b154d");'><span id='aa1f4f6a8aa54ff58481867d712b154d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1084')">1083-1084年</a>，42-43岁</div><div id='aa1f4f6a8aa54ff58481867d712b154d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年4月</a>　以信州从事得罢，入京师。作文。作品：张子厚睦州唱和集序。渡江集序。<div id='poem_1194125' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194125' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194125?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张子厚睦州唱和集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194125")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194125_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194125'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194125'>余友毗陵张子厚，出其《睦州唱和诗》一编曰：「为我序之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194125_comment'></div>余往年在大学，子厚尚未冠，其为诗，已有骏逸惊人之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194125_comment'></div>其后，学之益有所到，而弃官不就，归养于家，纵观群书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194125_comment'></div>与贤士大夫相上下，议论间，则虚弄笔墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194125_comment'></div>归为歌吟，纡徐曲折，穷古人之深处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194125_comment'></div>而与之应和者，又多东南之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194125_comment'></div>未几，得诗若干篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194125_comment'></div>夫诗之用于世久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194125_comment'></div>其言隐约，而出入于风谕比兴之间，使人可以喜，可以愠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194125_comment'></div>三代之际，会同燕享，必赋诗以见其志，所以察臧否，省祸福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194125_comment'></div>为国者，又以此占治乱，知兴亡，至于怨伤讥刺，道人情之所难言，而莫以为忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194125_comment'></div>后世风俗寖衰，士之克己好善者少，于是有因诗之一言而得罪于世者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194125_comment'></div>刘梦得弃置累年，白乐天谤及母子，凡坐此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194125_comment'></div>甚者父子相语，朋友相戒，曰诗不利于身，不可为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194125_comment'></div>是亦不善处之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194125_comment'></div>如子厚与诸君之作，优游乐易，摸写风物，自为嬉好，人亦知其不与世竞，读其言者，虽在朝市，而超然有汎江海入山林之心，方且皆喜慕称叹，欲追而从之，又何怨怒之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194125_comment'></div>余于是益知诗之不能为害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194125_comment'></div>元丰六年正月孔某序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1194125_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1194128' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194128' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194128?labeling=true' target='_blank'>渡江集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194128")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194128_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194128'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194128'>元丰六年，余以信州从事得罢，岁暮入京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194128_comment'></div>自九江驿至安上门，凡千六百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194128_comment'></div>自己亥至乙丑，凡二十七日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194128_comment'></div>时冬春之际，寒温交争，阴风怒号，霰雪横作，川草初茁，堤柳始芽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194128_comment'></div>蓝舆独行，无朋友谈笑之乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194128_comment'></div>邮舍孤寓，无子弟兼任之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194128_comment'></div>或长沙远水，极目无人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194128_comment'></div>或折椽败壁，卧见星斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194128_comment'></div>其荒寒閒寂，有常情不堪其忧者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194128_comment'></div>顾前后左右，无可告语，念非寄翰墨章句之间，无以散其郁湮而宽其寂寥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194128_comment'></div>故其览瞩风物，登涉山川，吊往念昔，感古怀今，以道途之蟠直险易，气象之风雨晦冥，发之于诗，叙而录之，得六十篇，以览观焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194128_comment'></div>是时，余四十有三年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194128_comment'></div>自始应举以至于今，六至阙下而三出江淮道以行，中间往还匆匆，经耳目如晡旦相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194128_comment'></div>而岁月数迁，时事屡变，吾家亲尊逝没，兄弟彫零，以区区嬴茧之身，寄食四海，南踰岭表，东至岱阳，而出入于江淮、荆湖、吴越之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194128_comment'></div>年三十有六，大病垂死，赖良医以得全活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194128_comment'></div>明年，以罪罢官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194128_comment'></div>此其出处险艰之大略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194128_comment'></div>盖二十五年之间，其变故之多如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194128_comment'></div>夫人之大数百年耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194128_comment'></div>方其少壮之时，筋力疲于奔走，精思涸于患难，其馀借有安乐饶泰，为日几何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194128_comment'></div>益知世之不足恃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194128_comment'></div>飞击潜游，以俟造化，惫而眠，饱而嬉，庶几不为达者之讥乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1194128_comment'></div>此皆吾诗不能悉载者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1194128_comment'></div>故并见之以自警云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1194128_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年4月</a>　在京师。曾巩卒，作祭文。作品：祭曾子固文。<div id='poem_1194216' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194216' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194216?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭曾子固文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194216")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194216_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194216'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194216'>惟公文为世表，识在人先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194216_comment'></div>愤道之息，志于必传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194216_comment'></div>绝众超群，自其少年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194216_comment'></div>况有宗工，援引于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194216_comment'></div>雷动风兴，声薄于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194216_comment'></div>匪独好古，穷探简编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194216_comment'></div>又达世务，不以迹牵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194216_comment'></div>潴为积泽，决为流泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194216_comment'></div>威为秋肃，施为春妍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194216_comment'></div>时辈谓公，德业之全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194216_comment'></div>外将六州，晚直西垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194216_comment'></div>商盘周诰，日代帝言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194216_comment'></div>枢庭钧府，众曰必迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194216_comment'></div>寿柄谁操，付与何偏？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194216_comment'></div>山摧玉折，反掌之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194216_comment'></div>士亡宗师，国失能贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194216_comment'></div>我少方蒙，公发其源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194216_comment'></div>长仕岱阴，从以周旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194216_comment'></div>决疑辨惑，一语不捐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194216_comment'></div>或钩其细，毫积丝联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194216_comment'></div>或究其大，苞方括圆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194216_comment'></div>面奖所是，夺其不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1194216_comment'></div>粗若有之，公赐多焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1194216_comment'></div>公方择隐，在湓之壖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1194216_comment'></div>我亦于此，谋安一廛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1194216_comment'></div>谓当优游，从容于田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1194216_comment'></div>幽明隔矣，所志不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1194216_comment'></div>茫茫太空，孰招以还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1194216_comment'></div>或当上浮，追蹑列仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1194216_comment'></div>决不没没，凡魂比肩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1194216_comment'></div>公名播后，不待铭镌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1194216_comment'></div>公子俱秀，当复大官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1194216_comment'></div>今当会哭，阻以山川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1194216_comment'></div>东南悠悠，不见新阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1194216_comment'></div>歛不造帷，窆不持棺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1194216_comment'></div>徒有伤悲，为涕涟涟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1194216_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1194216'></div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1194216_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年</a>　在京师，作文。作品：安堂记。田家坡赋。<div id='poem_1194176' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194176' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194176?labeling=true' target='_blank'>安堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年5月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194176")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194176_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194176'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194176'>朝奉郎太原王公出守上饶之初，更新约束，上下就序，决事以敏，行己以诚，惰者劝勉，奸者惩革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194176_comment'></div>未几，翕然称治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194176_comment'></div>乃为堂于使厅之后，曰安堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194176_comment'></div>客谓公曰：「天子躬亲万几，日旰而后食，询求良吏，付以远民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194176_comment'></div>以来治未久，奈何以安佚自处也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194176_comment'></div>曰：「非此之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194176_comment'></div>吾疾夫世之营营，而不安于分者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194176_comment'></div>欲守以为戒，且自勉也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194176_comment'></div>于是鲁国孔武仲为言其义曰：「天下之事，日接于人者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194176_comment'></div>利害荣辱之变，盛衰进退之序，循环如寒暑，迭至如昼夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194176_comment'></div>凡寓形于天地之间者，莫不由之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194176_comment'></div>而君子之所以异于众者，以能安之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194176_comment'></div>今夫茅茨为覆，上庳下湿，人以为不如雕墙华宇也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194176_comment'></div>断辕折轴，骖以款段，人以为不如朱轮驷马也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194176_comment'></div>穿绨为袍，败革为履，人以为不如锦衣赤舄也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194176_comment'></div>藜羹脱粟，每食不饱，人以为不如方丈五鼎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194176_comment'></div>以在彼为有馀，以在我为不足，疲心乏力以求之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194176_comment'></div>求不得，则怨且怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194176_comment'></div>幸而得之，未几何时，而复胜之者至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194176_comment'></div>于是与物竞逐，转至于无穷，往往冒宠邀利，而不知息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194176_comment'></div>或欲趋福，乃更速祸，岂不惑哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194176_comment'></div>君子明于此，是以修其在己者，朝夕不怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1194176_comment'></div>而其外来者，皆有以应之，而不留于胸中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1194176_comment'></div>其视富贵犹乘舟也，方其济川也，未尝不以舟也，已济则舍之，亦未尝眷眷于舟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1194176_comment'></div>其视贫贱，亦若此而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1194176_comment'></div>故朝为下士，暮为三公，不以为加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1194176_comment'></div>毁裂轩裳，退编白屋，不以为损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1194176_comment'></div>与之不喜，夺之不怨，惟其所遇，而不无自得焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1194176_comment'></div>其达也，若固有之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1194176_comment'></div>其穷也，我何憾于彼哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1194176_comment'></div>此古人之道德也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1194176_comment'></div>公才大名美，而门族之盛冠天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1194176_comment'></div>然不以贵势自骄，务推所学见于行事，治县佐州，闻誉大著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1194176_comment'></div>同时并游之人，或践历台省日久，或乘传持节出使四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1194176_comment'></div>循次而进，试一州于江湖绝远之地，在常情疑若未满，而公优游此堂，思所以修职业，报上恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1194176_comment'></div>宾客之至，清谈终日，而世俗之所慕者，无所累于其心，可谓贤矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1194176_comment'></div>武仲仕于此，公待之甚厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1194176_comment'></div>当纪夙迹，以告后人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1194176_comment'></div>况公之见属，乃不辞而为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1194176_comment'></div>元丰六年五月十九日也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1194176_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1193981' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1193981' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1193981?labeling=true' target='_blank'>田家坡赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年12月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1193981")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1193981_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1193981'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1193981'>登风冈以北望：山石嶙嶙而青白，非所谓两钟者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1193981_comment'></div>游气濛濛以薄天，非冯夷之所宫者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1193981_comment'></div>洪涛巨浪，号北风者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1193981_comment'></div>银山玉城，渺连宫者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1193981_comment'></div>昨余南归而至此，过钟石之旁畔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1193981_comment'></div>三江会而为一兮，浩联属乎天汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1193981_comment'></div>平沙不可以舣舟兮，凛惊肃其魂干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1193981_comment'></div>鸣两浆以横绝兮，寄宿夕于南岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1193981_comment'></div>舟人相戒以不寐兮，听城鼓而宵半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1193981_comment'></div>孤山岋其当前兮，闪群星之灿灿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1193981_comment'></div>及还吾乡，甫涉旬日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1193981_comment'></div>昔之川行，今则陆矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1193981_comment'></div>昔之舟处，今则屋矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1193981_comment'></div>欲舆而舆，欲马而马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1193981_comment'></div>入翱翔乎城邑，出驰骋乎坰野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1193981_comment'></div>险阻危厉，化为夷平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1193981_comment'></div>蛟龙无所用其威兮，江豚、白鱀安得以纵横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1193981_comment'></div>行持一筇，疲卧一石，而渴饮一觥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1193981_comment'></div>安得长此处兮，差优游以养生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1193981_comment'></div>涂于人之所不步兮，耘于人之所不耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1193981_comment'></div>顾谓仆者：「此何处也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1193981_comment'></div>对曰：「是名田家坡，去城十五里」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1193981_comment'></div>于时侧者御山，松声飕飗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1193981_comment'></div>溪塘湛其微波兮，梅花落而飞浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1193981_comment'></div>方旋辀而返辔，怅莫克以淹流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1193981_comment'></div>因援笔而成文，聊以识乎兹游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1193981_comment'></div>元丰六年十二月十三日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1193981_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　在京待选。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='9c0ad03c4ec74943b9a486b792939690_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9c0ad03c4ec74943b9a486b792939690");'><span id='9c0ad03c4ec74943b9a486b792939690_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1094')">1086-1094年</a>，45-53岁</div><div id='9c0ad03c4ec74943b9a486b792939690' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年3月</a>　三月，武仲自湘潭令赴秘书省正字召，自长沙舟行，八月始至京师，编途中所作诗为《丙寅赴阙诗稿》，有序。序。<div id='poem_1194126' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194126' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194126?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙寅赴阙诗藁序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194126")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194126_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194126'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194126'>元祐丙寅春，余自湘潭令为秘书省正字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194126_comment'></div>以力之不足于陆也，乃谋舟行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194126_comment'></div>盖自长沙至于京师，四十有二驿，赢粮秣马，期月而可至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194126_comment'></div>若夫水道则不然，乱重湖，沿大江，溯长淮，以入漕河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194126_comment'></div>春冬则浅涸断流，夏秋则淫潦极望，不幸而遭焉，有至于经月而踌躇，风起乎冥冥之间，拔山而贯天，大声虽息，而郁云未解，慒首而前，必有仓卒之惊，甚则覆溺之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194126_comment'></div>不幸而遇焉，则有至于踰旬而不进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194126_comment'></div>谚云：「迟者，速也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194126_comment'></div>篙工柁师，每以是见语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194126_comment'></div>余虽欲速达，至于此，则无以难之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194126_comment'></div>然自余之行，见覆舟者三矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194126_comment'></div>以谨慎，故幸免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194126_comment'></div>自三月至于八月，乃抵东水门外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194126_comment'></div>昨日，婢子持裌衣来曰：「寒将至矣，纩则未备」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194126_comment'></div>余愕曰：「是何炎凉之变，而岁月之奔驰耶」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194126_comment'></div>舟居迫逼无以自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194126_comment'></div>其间落日幽浦，平沙远岸，渔樵之下上，鸟鱼之升沉，时有旷然物外之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194126_comment'></div>登高临远，吊古人之遗迹，考之碑碣，问之耆老，记之本末，以备遗忘，则别录存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194126_comment'></div>其顾瞻啸嗷，模写风云，以寄一时之情状，则有诗赋若干篇在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194126_comment'></div>以余方官守于京师也，日驰于车辙马迹之间，幸朝廷宽大，时赐休告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194126_comment'></div>闭关一室，嚣然独坐，想见江湖风物，历历在耳目之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194126_comment'></div>得此二书者，出入相考，开卷而醒然，斯亦舒忧娱独之资也，于是次而藏之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1194126_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年3月29日</a>　任秘书省正字。作文。三月，弟平仲除知赣州军州事。作品：思养亭记。<div id='poem_1194179' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194179' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194179?labeling=true' target='_blank'>思养亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年3月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194179")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194179_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194179'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194179'>人子之事亲，承颜色，奉教令，先意谕道，凡亲之忧愉喜怒与其所嗜好，皆从容而得之，又致其敬焉，此之谓能养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194179_comment'></div>三日不怠，三月不懈，期悲哀，三年忧，终身慕，此之谓能思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194179_comment'></div>养者，致之于平昔之时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194179_comment'></div>思者，推之于既往之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194179_comment'></div>养有已焉，而思无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194179_comment'></div>今夫三岁之孺子，一日不见其亲，则僵仆啼号，不能自止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194179_comment'></div>及日月既久，稍忘其故习，于是笑语燕安，不异乎其常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194179_comment'></div>然则能思者，未必能久也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194179_comment'></div>夫能思其亲久而不衰者，其惟笃孝乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194179_comment'></div>春而雨露，见万物之敷荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194179_comment'></div>秋而繁霜，感草木之零落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194179_comment'></div>凡在天地之间者，皆得顺其性命以出入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194179_comment'></div>而吾亲今安归耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194179_comment'></div>于是设几席以象其居处，奏酒肴以象其饮食，以为亲虽不可得而见矣，陈其平日之所好乐，而致其爱慕之心，肃敬之容，则人子之眷眷，犹可以少伸于此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194179_comment'></div>寻阳张秉叔葬其母夫人于庐山之下，又作亭以备祭享，名之思养者，著其思亲之无已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194179_comment'></div>张氏世为南剑州人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194179_comment'></div>自太尉迁于江州，今四世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194179_comment'></div>衣冠而朝者，相继于位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194179_comment'></div>秉叔为人俊敏，尤明于道，屡为大邑，民悦附之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194179_comment'></div>余官于朝，而与之游且好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194179_comment'></div>亭成，见属为记，故为之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194179_comment'></div>夫人姓王氏，其世次德行，见于墓铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1194179_comment'></div>元祐元年三月二十九日，鲁国孔武仲记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1194179_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年5月2日</a>　自秘书省正字迁校书郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　任校书郎。有文。作品：谢校书陈学士启。萧贯之挂冠亭记。<div id='poem_1194051' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194051' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194051?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢校书陈学士启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194051")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194051_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194051'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194051'>伏审祗膺新命，入校秘文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194051_comment'></div>除目初传，士心咸悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194051_comment'></div>窃以西昆策府，典籍之所丛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194051_comment'></div>东观书林，英贤之攸萃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194051_comment'></div>网罗遗逸之彦，刊正谬说之传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194051_comment'></div>职业简清，龙光优渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194051_comment'></div>米盐细务，不至于耳目；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194051_comment'></div>朝廷要选，此为之权舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194051_comment'></div>宸极之旁，入而番直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194051_comment'></div>缙绅之旧，望若登仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194051_comment'></div>恭以某官志行清纯，矜露爽彻，学优前世之载，才适当今之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194051_comment'></div>早决上科，已积公卿之渐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194051_comment'></div>间随远牒，几忘轩冕之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194051_comment'></div>遂膺侧席之求，来集藏书之馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194051_comment'></div>牙签钿轴，慊施丹墨之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194051_comment'></div>金门玉堂，更蹑高华之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194051_comment'></div>辱珍函之见及，知谦德之有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194051_comment'></div>感愧之深，喻言莫悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1194051_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1194178' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194178' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194178?labeling=true' target='_blank'>萧贯之挂冠亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐元年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194178")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194178_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194178'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194178'>仕宦足慕耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194178_comment'></div>爵位通于朝，智策行于君，入则垂绅庙堂，出则持节方面，生有显名，没有美谥，人之情孰有睹是而不乐也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194178_comment'></div>然道之行否存乎时，名之美恶存乎人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194178_comment'></div>舍我之尺度而就彼之绳墨，遇则多忧，不遇则不乐，天机荡尽，而身亦随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194178_comment'></div>然则仕宦不足慕也，余之乡丈人萧公贯之，其深知此者与！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194178_comment'></div>公世家新喻，少以文章登进士上第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194178_comment'></div>历馆阁，屡为州使，年盛志得，有致君行道之资，而胸中浩然，不乐声利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194178_comment'></div>方其在京师时，已有诗十六篇，述江南四时风物之美，以未得即归为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194178_comment'></div>则公之意，岂胶于一官而不去哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194178_comment'></div>既又营其居舍之东，将因以筑亭，为退归燕息之所，命之曰挂冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194178_comment'></div>公之年止于四十有六，而亭亦未及为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194178_comment'></div>其子潜夫，即其居而屋之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194178_comment'></div>间与宾客谈笑其上，视其湍石之清激曰：「此吾先君之所欲钓而未暇也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194178_comment'></div>顾其花木之幽深曰：「此吾先君之手植而将徘徊其间也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194178_comment'></div>士大夫多为诗赋，而潜夫属余为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194178_comment'></div>余为之慨然曰：「人之遽旋于天地之间，俄顷耳！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194178_comment'></div>耳目之过也，不须臾留，而人之寿，又有短长不可计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194178_comment'></div>古之英豪，郁其所蕴积，而赍恨于冥冥者，多以此也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194178_comment'></div>贯之之没，今五十年，天下之人皆知其可用之才，而未必知其高尚之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194178_comment'></div>非有子，其能追迹而显扬之与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194178_comment'></div>于是，又知潜夫之贤也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194178_comment'></div>元祐元年七月二十七日，鲁国孔武仲记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1194178_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年7月</a>　任校书郎。有诗。作品：送苏迈尉酸枣。<span class='inlineComment2'>（据《苏辙年谱》（孔凡礼著，学苑出版社二〇〇一年）。）</span><div id='poem_58441' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58441' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58441?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送苏迈尉酸枣</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58441")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_58441_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58441'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58441'>酷暑日逾退，凉风生早秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58441'>翩翩苏公子，一官不远游。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58441'>仕养两得意，人生复何求。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58441'>骏马如飞星，锦带垂吴钩。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58441'>到邑嚚讼少，官闲吏兵休。<div id='poem_sentence_4_58441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_58441'>还当有佳吟，吟到黄河头。<div id='poem_sentence_5_58441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_58441'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_58441_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　任校书郎。有文。作品：元祐召试馆职记。<div id='poem_1194184' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194184' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194184?labeling=true' target='_blank'>元祐召试馆职记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194184")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194184_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194184'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194184'>盛矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194184_comment'></div>元祐之初也，圣贤相遭，上下顺治，刑省兵息，徭轻赋平，德泽浃乎宇内矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194184_comment'></div>天子曰：「嘻，惟祖宗之所维驭天下，传之无穷者，何尝不以降儒学为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194184_comment'></div>故太祖亲崇文之馆，神考复书省之制，藏在策府，为后世观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194184_comment'></div>顾予纂业之始，天下向风，宜有以宠嘉贤士大夫」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194184_comment'></div>乃命大臣司马公以下七人，各举其所知以闻，皆召试玉堂，问以为治之大要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194184_comment'></div>修校理之废，因校书正字之旧，以序厥位，而四方之英才，杂遝阙下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194184_comment'></div>于是在是选者，咸知庙廷所以期之者，其意远非特调朱黄，是正文字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194184_comment'></div>而林居巷隐，幽绝荒徼之人，父讯子，兄饬弟，以朝廷待士无有亲疏迩远，日勉学行，庶几为上所收用，其劝励风俗，不已博乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194184_comment'></div>夫人之才否，无有定分，惟上所以器之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194184_comment'></div>论思献纳之任，不可一日旷于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194184_comment'></div>及人才之少，乃求之于庶位之中，是犹金玉绮绣不贮于家，而一旦索之于市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194184_comment'></div>欲其精粹，不可得已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194184_comment'></div>此贤才不可不素养，而君相所以深谋于上也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194184_comment'></div>余方校书省中，睹同舍之盛，以为法度因革之初，可以传于久者，不可以无志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194184_comment'></div>乃录其姓氏名字，及其论荐所出于左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194184_comment'></div>凡十六人云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1194184_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年9月</a>　任校书郎。九月丙朔，司马光卒，武仲有挽诗。作品：司马温公挽诗。<div id='poem_58101' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58101' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58101")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58101_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58101'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58101'>龙卧南阳久，天回北斗高。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58101'>庙堂更政化，岩谷起英髦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58101_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58100' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58100' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58100?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58100_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58100'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58100'>鼎鼐华元老，朝廷倚上台。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58100'>除疴得针砭，作解有风雷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58100'>尚冀松椿寿，谁令柱石摧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58100'>英灵参列宿，馀惠在春台。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58100'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58100_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58099' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58099' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58099?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58099_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58099'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58099'>赐告恩稠叠，闻丧上震惊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58099'>秋原无喜色，夜雨有悲声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58097'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58097_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　任校书郎。作文。作品：宋岳州平冈县王文正公祠堂碑。<div id='poem_1194203' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194203' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194203?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋岳州平江县王文正公祠堂碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194203")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194203_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194203'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194203'>岳州平江县，故丞相王文正公所尝治也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194203_comment'></div>旧有公祠堂，岁久寖敝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194203_comment'></div>治平元年，知县事张仲舒迁于宝积寺，以公之没，更历四朝，而民奉事如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194203_comment'></div>公讳旦，字子明，大名莘人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194203_comment'></div>太平兴国五年登进士第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194203_comment'></div>授大理评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194203_comment'></div>天子加恤远方，为亲择县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194203_comment'></div>是岁，公承命以来，为政简明，百姓安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194203_comment'></div>及其去，老幼遮道涕泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194203_comment'></div>公为人静默，不干时誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194203_comment'></div>久之，近臣荐其才，乃归朝，以文章登侍从，卒致位丞相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194203_comment'></div>秉国之政十有八年，天下乂安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194203_comment'></div>公之泽被四海，而兹邑之人，德公尤深，宜其尸而祠之，虽久而不忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194203_comment'></div>曾孙古贤，闻于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194203_comment'></div>元祐元年，奉使湖南，追感其家世，且见谓曰：「开宝中，晋公出守长沙，至太宗时，文正为县湖北，父子继踵于湖湘之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194203_comment'></div>小子不敏，复备位于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194203_comment'></div>而文正祠不大显，宜有碑铭，揭之后世，愿以属于子」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194203_comment'></div>武仲尝考近时名臣之迹，得公之遗事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194203_comment'></div>谓公功业宜为王者相，道义宜为学者师，恨不及识公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194203_comment'></div>闻公之像，实在近境，欲一拜于堂下未能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194203_comment'></div>诚得载名公碑，以自托于不朽，其又何辞，乃为之述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194203_comment'></div>而继以诗曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1194203'>自昔为相，先试治民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1194203_comment'></div>非但人事，天意或然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1194203_comment'></div>商周之师，钓渭耕莘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1194203_comment'></div>涉历险阻，知民艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1194203_comment'></div>及其见用，利泽加人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1194203_comment'></div>龙之将升，亦泥于蟠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1194203_comment'></div>朋蛇侣螾，蓄智潜神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1194203_comment'></div>雷风相趋，遂济丰年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1194203_comment'></div>惟文正公，之孝之忠，之量之才，之勋之庸，卓大深长，群臣之宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1194203_comment'></div>天子仰之，惟公议从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1194203_comment'></div>元首股肱，始卒一躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1194203_comment'></div>号称太平，三代是同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1194203_comment'></div>太湖之滨，今有公宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1194203_comment'></div>昔公宰是，惠及纤洪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1194203_comment'></div>肇自百里，施于万邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1194203_comment'></div>其遇也时，其进从容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1194203_comment'></div>勒之坚珉，以告无穷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1194203_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年1月</a>　任校书郎。与黄庭坚唱和。黄庭坚有《常父惠示丁卯雪十四韵谨同韵赋之》。作品：丁卯春雪呈同僚。<span class='inlineComment2'>（黄庭坚是岁在秘书省兼史局，正月除著作郎。）</span><div id='poem_58332' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58332' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58332?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丁卯春雪呈同僚</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58332")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_58332_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58332'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58332'>经时无甘泽，帝为元元忧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58332'>新正得一雪，尚可期有秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58332'>狂风<span class='inlineComment2'>（豫章本作风声）</span>东北来，浩浩举山丘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58332'>飞霰为先驱，繁英已绸缪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58332'>堆深地欲蛰，舞急川争流。<div id='poem_sentence_4_58332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_58332'>沉沉西崦暮，落势漫不收。<div id='poem_sentence_5_58332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_58332'>尽移白玉京，来为帝王州。<div id='poem_sentence_6_58332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_58332'>疠鬼窘相泣，凄凉苦罢休。<div id='poem_sentence_7_58332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_58332'>旱魃亦失气，耿耿空自囚。<div id='poem_sentence_8_58332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_58332'>从兹民其康，终岁饱麦麰。<div id='poem_sentence_9_58332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_58332'>端门盛佳气，策府多英游。<div id='poem_sentence_10_58332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_58332'>谅多赞时瑞，岂独吟空愁。<div id='poem_sentence_11_58332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_58332'>金樽发清扬，思涌如云浮。<div id='poem_sentence_12_58332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_58332'>请歌丰年占，以代击壤讴。<div id='poem_sentence_13_58332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_58332'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_58332_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年2月</a>　任校书郎。二月，弟平仲为集贤校理。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　任校书郎。与刘颁、苏轼、曾肇等唱和。苏轼诗《次韵三舍人省上》，苏辙有《次韵孔武仲三舍人省上》，作品：三舍人题名于后省试皆赋诗因寄呈刘贡父。<span class='inlineComment2'>（三舍人指曾子开、刘贡父、孔经父，皆江西人。）</span>曾子开示诗再用前韵。苏子由示诗再用前韵。<div id='poem_58337' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58337' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58337?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三舍人题名于后省皆赋诗因寄呈刘贡父</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58337")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_58337_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58337'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58337'>西垣寂寞今已久，三贤文章凤池手。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58337_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58337'>朝来不复恋山中，后至傥谁居客右。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58337_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58337'>华堂刻石映今古，秀句连章动星斗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58337_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58337'>鸰原棣萼俱相望，龙吟虎啸生辉光。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58337_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58337'>就中贡父我<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>故乡，况有小阮争翱翔，翩翩亦试中书堂。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58337_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_58337'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_58337_0'>⑴ 原缺，据豫章本补</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_58337_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_58493' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58493' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58493?labeling=true' target='_blank'>曾子开示诗再用前韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58493")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_58493_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58493'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58493'>川滔海积岁月久，书秃十毫未停手。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58493_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58493'>昔人四十夸专城，公佩黄金来帝右。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58493_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58493'>当年逸足起江西，时辈共喜星之斗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58493_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58493'>荣华未满众所望，天启叔季侍清光。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58493_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58493'>莫言昼锦归故乡，莫对秋雁思南翔，且登金门上玉堂。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58493_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>苏子由示诗再用前韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58406")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_58406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58406'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58406'>公家两贤涉世久，六马从容辔在手。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58406'>驱驰有节心有常，进退不随人左右。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58406'>十年挫抑心不回，方知有胆大如斗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58406'>鸾坡凤阁蔚相望，灿灿奎壁连晶光。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58406'>我家辛勤出寒乡，斥鴳未易追翱翔，莫将沧溟比坳堂。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58406_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年4月30日</a>　任校书郎。顾临赴河北路都转运使，文仲等为其饯行并有序。作品：送顾子敦赴河北序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（文仲有《四月三十日慈孝寺山亭席上口占送子敦都运待制赴河北》，黄庭坚有《次韵子瞻送顾子敦河北都运二首》、《饯子敦席上奉同孔经父八韵》，苏轼有《送顾子敦奉使河朔》、《诸公饯子敦轼以病不往复次前韵》，范祖禹有《四月三十日慈孝寺山亭席上次韵经父舍人送子敦都运待制赴河北》，刘攽有《慈孝寺送顾待制次韵和孔舍人》平仲《孔氏谈苑》卷二《顾将军》条：“元祐二年，辛雍自光禄丞移太常博士，顾子敦自给事中除河朔漕，付以治河，京师语曰：‘治礼已差辛博士，修河仍用顾将军。’子敦好谈兵，人谓之顾将军也。”）</span><div id='poem_1194122' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194122' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194122?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送顾子敦使河北序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年4月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194122")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194122_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194122'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194122'>上之二年，顾公子敦自河东转运使召给事中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194122_comment'></div>天下方向太平之治，褒采群言，以广视听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194122_comment'></div>子敦在门下，事有不便，辄争还之，议论坚决，不少迎合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194122_comment'></div>是时，河北数有水灾，澶魏故道，久湮未复，议臣纷然，计有未定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194122_comment'></div>子敦日日语人曰：「此不难办也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194122_comment'></div>昔大禹浚九川，陂九泽，以一人之经营，而及万世，盖亲见而力行之耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194122_comment'></div>语闻，即日拜天章阁待制使河北，俾条便宜，悉以来上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194122_comment'></div>士大夫藉藉交语，以为侍从之官所论者，天下之事也，河为数州之患，虽急，一方之事也，子敦以侍从之官，辄而使一方，忽所大而治所小，非计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194122_comment'></div>然子敦不为变志动心，朝廷不为易辞反令者，朝廷知体，而子敦知务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194122_comment'></div>夫河之为中国患久矣，今近尤为汗漫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194122_comment'></div>自小吴之决，息、冀、深、洺之民，鸟惊兽骇，炊不暇暖釜，饮未及濡唇，而原野一旦化为平流矣，是天下之大变也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194122_comment'></div>夫以天下之大变，而当圣主勤政急治之时，其谋度施为，宜何如也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194122_comment'></div>而以常情疑之，陋矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194122_comment'></div>子敦自少喜论兵，以孙武、诸葛为师法，时人咸谓才堪将帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194122_comment'></div>及西方用师，天子之士，争以军谋战法进取于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194122_comment'></div>子敦深藏远引，默默若无能者，知兵之未可用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194122_comment'></div>已而师出无效，子敦之智益明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194122_comment'></div>今河之害，可谓大矣，举朝之人，睥睨前却，不敢径往以蹈后悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194122_comment'></div>子敦独日夜计画，以为己任，非确然不惑，其肯为之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194122_comment'></div>余于是为河北之人贺曰：顾公来，若等可以安坐而食，高枕而卧矣！</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1194122_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年5月</a>　任校书郎。兄文仲自朝奉郎、起居舍人拜左谏议大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年7月</a>　任校书郎。武仲有诗送张商英提刑河东。作品：送天觉使河东。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《续资治通鉴长编》卷四〇三：“张商英元祐二年七月由开封出为河东提刑。）</span><div id='poem_58209' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58209' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58209?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送天觉使河东</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58209")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年11月26日</a>　任校书郎。十一月甲戌，兄孔文仲由左谏议大夫任中书舍人。十一月，弟孔平仲为秘书丞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　任校书郎。与苏辙、苏轼唱和。苏辙有《次韵孔武仲学士见赠》，苏轼有《见子由与孔常父唱和诗，辄次其韵。余在馆中，同舍出入，辄相聚饮酒赋诗。近岁不复讲，故终篇及之，庶几诸公稍复其旧，亦太平盛事也》诗。作品：答苏子由留赠。<div id='poem_58506' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　任校书郎。孔宗翰卒，武仲有挽词。作品：孔周翰挽词三首。<div id='poem_58087' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58087' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58087'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58087'>邂逅湓江口，方知叔父亲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58087'>荣华才一梦，奄忽几千春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58087'>白玉沽何晚，精金锻愈真。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58087'>耆年所宜得，天苦夺斯人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58087'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58087_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58086' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58086' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_58086_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58086'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58086'>循吏今之选，皇华使者轺。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58086'>关河初异路，巾笏偶同朝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58086'>急景催迟莫，清魂返泬寥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58086'>一哀惭不达，生理故风飙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58086'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58086_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58085' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58085' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58085?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58085_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58085'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58085'>晚岁班朝列，光华动士林。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58085_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58085'>家风当冠豸，官序正腰金。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58085_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58085'>霄汉亨衢浅，膏肓积沴深。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58085_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58085'>凄凉哭门馆，笑语尚馀音。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58085_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58085'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58085_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　任校书郎。武仲骑马访苏轼，有诗和答。苏轼有《偶与客饮孔常父见访方设席延请忽上马驰去已而有诗戏用其韵答之》。作品：谒苏子瞻因记。<div id='poem_58484' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58484' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58484?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谒苏子瞻因寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58484")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_58484_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58484'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58484'>华严长者貌古奇，紫瞳奕奕双眉垂<span class='inlineComment2'>（豫章本作烨烨双秀眉）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58484'>颜如桃花两侍儿，问其姓名自不知。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58484'>嗫嚅欲吐新奇词，岂亦有虎来护持。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58484'>维摩高卧尽不应，蓬山藏史策马驰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58484'>三豪兀坐浑如痴，错认醍醐是酒卮，谁将此景付画师。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58484_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　任校书郎。武仲赋苏轼所画怪石。作品：东坡居士画怪石赋。<div id='poem_1193984' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1193984' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1193984?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东坡居士画怪石赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1193984")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1193984_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1193984'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1193984'>东坡居士壮长多难，而处乎江湖之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1193984_comment'></div>或夕休于岩，或朝饷于野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1193984_comment'></div>或钓于水之滨，或耕于山之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1193984_comment'></div>颀然八尺，皆知其为异人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1193984_comment'></div>观于万物，无所不适，而尤得意于怪石之嶙峋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1193984_comment'></div>或凌烟而孤起，或绝渚而罗陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1193984_comment'></div>端庄丑怪，不可以悉状也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1193984_comment'></div>苍苍黮黮，碨碨礧礧，森森以鳞鳞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1193984_comment'></div>彼造物者何简也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1193984_comment'></div>此赋形者何多也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1193984_comment'></div>盖含之为一气，散之为万物，非尺度所裁量，斧凿所增损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1193984_comment'></div>乃知夫黜聪明，捐智巧，则其动作固将有凝于神也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1193984_comment'></div>乃濡秃毫，阐幽思，以心虚为无象，以感触为太始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1193984_comment'></div>混沌黔娄，左右为之相；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1193984_comment'></div>浮立洪崖，唯诺为之使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1193984_comment'></div>移瞬息于千年，托方寸于万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1193984_comment'></div>其醉墨淋漓，藏于人家，散于塔庙者，盖有年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1193984_comment'></div>一日止前驺，款荆关，解金龟，置紫绶，而苍颜瘦骨，杰焉如长松之临岁寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1193984_comment'></div>举酒而屡釂，仰屋而独言曰：「吾之胸中若有嵬峨突兀，欲出而未肆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1193984_comment'></div>又若嵩高太华，乍隐乍显」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1193984_comment'></div>在乎窗户之下，几案之前，乘兴命童奴展纸万幅，浇歙溪之石，磨隃麋之丸，睥睨八荒，运移云烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1193984_comment'></div>不知太山之覆于左，麋鹿之兴于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1193984_comment'></div>亦不知我之在此，而人之旁观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1193984_comment'></div>一挥而皴苍菌蠢之体具，再抚而幽深杳远之意足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1193984_comment'></div>如在武昌之麓，二别之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1193984_comment'></div>是时朔风号怒，寒气充斥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1193984_comment'></div>日临西云，倒射东壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1193984_comment'></div>居士既得其象，又感其声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1193984_comment'></div>写修纤与森蔚，横斜出乎峥嵘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1193984_comment'></div>悄乎如鸟雀之将下，泠然若幽泉之可听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1193984_comment'></div>乃有霜腮铁面百岁之翁，瞪若有睹，卷之怀中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1193984_comment'></div>居士无吝色，无矜容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1193984_comment'></div>淡若亡也，岂以为彼取之有限，我应之不穷！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1193984_comment'></div>尝闻之曰：「文者，无形之画；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1193984_comment'></div>画者，有形之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1193984_comment'></div>二者异迹而同趋，以其皆能传生写似，为世之所贵珍」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1193984_comment'></div>居士之文，俟伟闳博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1193984_comment'></div>纡馀姣好矣，而又欲穷丹青之妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1193984_comment'></div>忧以此娱情，欢以此寓笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1193984_comment'></div>盖将以贾谊、陆贽之辞，凯之、摩诘之笔，兼之乎一身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1193984_comment'></div>故其动之为风，散之为云，敛之为秋，舒之为春，是何其视听食息与我略均，而多才与艺如此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1193984_comment'></div>此余之所以心醉乎斯人也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1193984_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　任校书郎。武仲赋苏轼所画枯木。作品：子瞻画枯木。<div id='poem_58344' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58344' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58344?labeling=true' target='_blank'>子瞻画枯木</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58344")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_58344_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58344'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58344'>寒云行空乱春华，西风凛凛空吹沙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58344'>夫子抱膝若丧魄，谁知巧思中萌芽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58344'>败毫淡墨任挥染，苍莽菌蠢移龙蛇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58344'>略增点缀已成就，止见枯木成槎枒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58344'>更无丹青相掩翳，惟有口鼻随穿呀。<div id='poem_sentence_4_58344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_58344'>往年江湖饱观画<span class='inlineComment2'>（豫章本作觇眺）</span>，或在山隈溪水涯。<div id='poem_sentence_5_58344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_58344'>腹中空洞夜藏魅，巅顶突兀春无花。<div id='poem_sentence_6_58344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_58344'>径深最宜系画舸，日落时复停归鸦。<div id='poem_sentence_7_58344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_58344'>苏公早与俗子偶，避世欲种东陵瓜。<div id='poem_sentence_8_58344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_58344'>窥观尽得物外趣，移向纸上无毫差。<div id='poem_sentence_9_58344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_58344'>醉中遗落不秘惜，往往流传<span class='inlineComment2'>（豫章本作落）</span>藏人家。<div id='poem_sentence_10_58344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_58344'>赵昌丹青最细<span class='inlineComment2'>（豫章本作匀）</span>腻，直与春色争豪华。<div id='poem_sentence_11_58344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_58344'>公今好尚何太癖，曾载木车出岷巴。<div id='poem_sentence_12_58344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_58344'>轻肥欲与世为戒，未许木叶胜枯槎。<div id='poem_sentence_13_58344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_58344'>万物流形若泫露，百岁俄惊眼如车。<div id='poem_sentence_14_58344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_58344'>树犹如此不长久，人以何者堪矜誇。<div id='poem_sentence_15_58344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_58344'>悠悠坐见死生境，但随天机无损加。<div id='poem_sentence_16_58344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_58344'>却笑金城对宫柳，泫然流涕空咨嗟。<div id='poem_sentence_17_58344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_58344'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_58344_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　任校书郎。作黄好谦挽词。作品：黄几道挽词。<div id='poem_58278' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58278' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58278?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黄几道挽词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span id='poem_sentence_0_58278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58278'>诗社苦吟霜月白，离亭纵饮酒杯空。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年7月</a>　任校书郎。七月，周尹知梓州，武仲有诗送之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年9月</a>　充集贤校理。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年9月</a>　任集贤校理。武仲送曹辅赴闽中，有诗。作品：送曹子方奉使闽中。<div id='poem_58447' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58447' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58447?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送曹千方奉使闽中</a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58447")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58447_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58447'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58447'>闻说乘轺美，全□胜赴□<span class='inlineComment2'>（豫章本作胜赴□□）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58447'>先声驰岭海，和气入山川。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年3月20日</a>　任著作佐郎。与李周等十八人集会于信安公之园亭。作文。作品：信安公园亭题名记。<div id='poem_1194183' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194183' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194183?labeling=true' target='_blank'>信安公园亭题名记</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐五年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194183")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194183_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194183'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194183'>五代之际，豪杰割裂疆土，自为侯王，九州之人，寄息鼎镬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194183_comment'></div>乱极而治，生我太祖，起布衣，践宸极，将天之威，整肃四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194183_comment'></div>弱国纳土，强者缚面，而江南君臣，犹负固自若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194183_comment'></div>太祖曰：「彼其所以崛强沮泽之间，引活岁月者，以有长江之险为可恃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194183_comment'></div>吾有道使彼舟楫无所用其巧，则全吴地千里可旦夕平也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194183_comment'></div>乃命度国西空旷之地，辟士潴泉，规以为池，外引京索之水以益之，渊容海滀，一旦成就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194183_comment'></div>陈楼船，习战士，步水如陆，操舟如车，吴人闻之，气索胆碎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194183_comment'></div>及旌旗南指，州邑瓦解厥角，稽首请命下吏，而江表平矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194183_comment'></div>天下无事，干戈藏于库，军旅休于屯，中州之人，日益富庶安乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194183_comment'></div>向之讲武处，遂为游集最盛之地，时变使然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194183_comment'></div>若其雕甍屈槛隐见波底，长桥穹殿翔绝霄外，清来午风，阴却晡暑，则唐之曲江也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194183_comment'></div>草木润茂，洲渚重沓，鱼龙之所兴伏，日月之所出没，则汉之昆明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194183_comment'></div>暮春之月，锦绣夺目，车驺填道，倾坊空巷，旦朝而出游，鼓鼙振野，笙箫顺耳，日暮而忘归，则洛阳之曲水也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194183_comment'></div>羽者飞于上，鳞者潜于下，和气之所薰蒸，仁风之所衣被，莫不自得焉，则镐京之灵沼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194183_comment'></div>中天下之大而都之，总前王之美而有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194183_comment'></div>以亲见而测传闻，则史牒之所称诧，赋颂之所叹咏，未易相先后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194183_comment'></div>七圣袭沿，清净简默，池去阙庭才十许里，而率十年间不一再至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194183_comment'></div>然而陈龙舟，出水嬉，作鼓吹，调厩马，常若车驾亲临其上者，凡以推至上与民同乐之心，而为都人娱心属目之盛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194183_comment'></div>夫内不辍朝廷听治之勤，外不废都人酺醵之逸，约己裕人，可谓兼之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194183_comment'></div>自祖宗优遇馆阁，岁出后苑御库酒以赐之，于是有池上之集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194183_comment'></div>元祐五年三月乙酉，太平王仲至以秘书少监实领兹会，修故事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194183_comment'></div>于是宿戒宾客，晨出西郊，同舍皆集于琼林苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1194183_comment'></div>既又泛舟池中，环水殿后，循桥而北，骑而适信安公之园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1194183_comment'></div>宴语至暮，相与涵泳恩思，歌吟太平，为一时之盛游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1194183_comment'></div>又以为席中之人，合散不常，异时复来，则其先后出处之详，宜有以考也，乃题姓名壁间以志之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1194183_comment'></div>在是会者：李周纯之、盛侨晦之、王钦臣仲至、杜常正夫、崔公度伯昌、陈蔡诚老、盛次仲居中、林旦次中、李德刍质夫、宋匪躬履中、孔武仲彦常、黄裳冕仲、刘唐老会臣、李昭玘成季、徐铎振甫、晁补之无咎、张耒文潜，韩治循之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1194183_comment'></div>以事不至者：黄廉夷仲、吴安许传正、孙朴元忠、黄庭坚鲁直、元耆宁台寿、司马原公材、余中行老概、仲平、廖正一明略。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1194183_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年3月29日</a>　除国子司业，具状辞免。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年9月</a>　任国子司业兼侍讲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年1月9日</a>　任国子司业兼侍讲。权知贡举。是时韦骧有《同文馆试上舍和同事孔彦常学士即事》、《又和》、《又和前韵呈彦常明叔》、《又和彦常试院即事》诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年4月20日</a>　任国子司业兼侍讲。四月三十日，平仲充秘阁校理、提点江浙铸钱。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年7月8日</a>　自集贤校理、国子司业兼侍讲除起局郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年11月23日</a>　除中书舍人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年11月24日</a>　任中书舍人，因工部侍郎王钦臣十八日为给事中，二十四日武仲缴奏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年11月</a>　任中书舍人，廖正一除秘阁代理，武仲举以自代。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年12月</a>　任中书舍人，武仲奏荐仙韶副使胥氏可充乐正管仙韶公事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年4月</a>　任中书舍人。礼部侍郎兼侍讲范祖禹进《荐讲读官札子》荐武仲进讲读。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年4月19日</a>　任中书舍人。有诗。作品：宋岳州平江县王文正公祠堂记。<div id='poem_1194172' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194172' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194172?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋岳州平江县王文正公祠堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1092年4月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194172")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194172_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194172'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194172'>故丞相王文正公旦，尝知岳之平江，有善政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194172_comment'></div>公既去，其民相与筑堂画像而祠之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194172_comment'></div>其后，栋宇敝阙，则奉公之像宝积佛舍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194172_comment'></div>久之，宝积燔于火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194172_comment'></div>县人复相与谋曰：「我公去此虽久，而泽之被于民者尚在也，而可以遂忘乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194172_comment'></div>乃求公所尝游息之地，得县西之山元老亭，即而祠焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194172_comment'></div>自公之去，更历五朝，凡百有馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194172_comment'></div>当时父老，皆无在者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194172_comment'></div>敝之以风雨，蜚之以烈焰，地三易矣，而人心不移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194172_comment'></div>此岂号令约束之所及哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194172_comment'></div>盖德之在人者深，而人之怀公者至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194172_comment'></div>黄发之叟，垂髫之童，语以相传，无有终极，虽千万世如今日可也，况十百年之间乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194172_comment'></div>公始以文学识度见知于真宗皇帝，遂登相位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194172_comment'></div>秉国政十有八年，天下富乐，四夷宾服，视汉唐间所谓甚盛之时，未有过之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194172_comment'></div>是时，国家閒暇，天子以盛德兴礼乐，以几唐虞三代之治，文武并用，贤能辈出，其议论倜傥，功名暴著者，络绎于图史之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194172_comment'></div>然术业遐远，使人心服者，无与公比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194172_comment'></div>以真宗之圣，而得公之贤，道合志同，不言而心喻，优游岩廊，以至太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194172_comment'></div>故其德行勋庸，载于策书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194172_comment'></div>虽以田野之耆老，皆能知公之名，道公之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194172_comment'></div>儒生学士，以公之功德拟于前世，汉则魏、丙，晋则王、谢，唐则房、杜，而未有以为溢美者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194172_comment'></div>至公论宰相之器，安閒静密，能使大事为小，有事为无者，必以公为法，未有闻之而不悦服者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194172_comment'></div>此犹功成名立之后，朝廷之所褒，史臣之所称叹，既以浃熟于天下之耳目矣，故其知之不难，其信之不易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1194172_comment'></div>若公在平江时，齿少位卑，言动束于上下之势，施为阻于法令之禁，其泽未广也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1194172_comment'></div>其受诏而至，岁满而罢，与吏民接者三年之顷耳，其居未久也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1194172_comment'></div>而其人歌咏爱慕，至今与公始去之时无异，其拜俯奉事之严，如公之在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1194172_comment'></div>是果何术以致之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1194172_comment'></div>尝闻久而不可变者，莫如诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1194172_comment'></div>诚之所加，大可以动天地，幽可以感鬼神，其力可以回寒暑，其精可以裂金石，而况于民与我同类者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1194172_comment'></div>然则公之所以得民者，其事无穷，而其理可以一言尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1194172_comment'></div>公之曾孙古，奉使湖南，余客长沙，欲余记其事以示久远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1194172_comment'></div>其后七年，并官于朝，间而见语曰：「卒无以扬我祖之德乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1194172_comment'></div>余以谓公之事业在于天下，传于众人，诚不待论著而后明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1194172_comment'></div>然被之金石，以贻无穷，所以佐荆人之思，且明公之所以为宋宗臣者，其端乃在人未知之时，非已贵而后为之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1194172_comment'></div>则后之人瞻仰馀烈，而欲企及之者，当如何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1194172_comment'></div>故为之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1194172_comment'></div>元祐七年四月十九日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1194172_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年8月24日</a>　任中书舍人。武仲檄宋用臣词头。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年8月</a>　任中书舍人。有奏。作品：上哲宗乞轮侍从官进对奏。<div id='poem_1194021' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194021' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194021?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞轮侍从官进对奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐七年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194021")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194021_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194021'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194021'>臣伏见前日近臣论奏乞罢侍从官转对，而专责以朝夕论思之效，朝廷寻已施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194021_comment'></div>臣以谓论思者，侍从之事，然苟不持之以法度，则责无所归，言与不言，各从其意，论思之要，果安在也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194021_comment'></div>昔唐太宗闻直谏则奖励之，久不言则诮薄之，风声所感，郡下自励，是以终贞观之世，中外无壅蔽之事，朝廷无佞媚之臣，政理之效，优出近世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194021_comment'></div>仁宗皇帝尝御正阳门，亲策群臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194021_comment'></div>又尝开天章阁，召执政八人赐坐，授以纸笔，使条陈政事之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194021_comment'></div>尝谓辅臣曰：「近日上封言政事得失何其少也，岂非言路壅塞所致乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194021_comment'></div>英宗皇帝谓范纯仁曰：「近日风俗可嘉，群臣罢朝，屡来言事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194021_comment'></div>如此，人君日有益矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194021_comment'></div>仁宗、英宗汲汲求人言如此，是以至和、嘉祐、治平之政，至今称颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194021_comment'></div>昨日陛下亲御经筵，许讲读官进对，凡预讲读者，不过五六人，陛下闻其规戒之言亦多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194021_comment'></div>况侍从官不止五六人，其言天下之事者固多，患在未有以率之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194021_comment'></div>伏望远稽唐太宗及仁宗、英宗勤求人言之义，近推经筵许侍臣进对之意，轮流侍从官二人进对，令各陈所见，择其是者推行之，则转对之法虽废，而论思之责犹在也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1194021_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年8月</a>　任中书舍人。仲秋，武仲曝书，有诗。张耒、黄裳、秦观有诗相和。作品：壬申仲秋与东观曝书之会谨赋五言四韵律诗一首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（张耒有《次韵孔舍人曝书》，黄裳有《次常父著作曝书之韵》、秦观有《次韵孔彦常舍人曝书》）</span><div id='poem_58356' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58356' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58356?labeling=true' target='_blank'>壬申仲秋与东观曝书之会谨赋五言四韵律诗一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1092年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58356")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58356_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58356'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58356'>秋风解烦暑，尊俎可从容。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58356'>尽会青云士，来游群玉峰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58356'>琅函窥一一，金钥发重重。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58356'>四库传观喜，惟应吏困供。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58356'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58356_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年9月</a>　任中书舍人。武仲等议请南郊专祀上帝而间以孟冬诣北郊亲祠。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年10月</a>　以中书舍人兼直学士院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年</a>　任中书舍人。弟平仲提点京西路刑狱公事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年2月4日</a>　任中书舍人，有奏。作品：乞罢唐义问知广州奏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年3月26日</a>　武仲自中书舍人迁给事中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年4月4日</a>　武仲自给事中迁礼部侍郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年12月29日</a>　任礼部侍郎，有咏雪诗，韦骧唱和。作品：癸酉腊雪。<span class='inlineComment2'>（韦骧有《和孔彦常侍郎癸酉冬雪》。）</span>癸酉冬雪。<span class='inlineComment2'>（韦骧有《和孔彦常侍郎癸酉冬雪》。）</span><div id='poem_58204' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58204' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58204?labeling=true' 谷城（穀城）

<div class='label1' id='aed7ee3fc17a4876a6ba0dcd05d31830_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("aed7ee3fc17a4876a6ba0dcd05d31830");'><span id='aed7ee3fc17a4876a6ba0dcd05d31830_link'
