ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　任穀城主簿。是年弟平仲为国学解魁，有《国学解元谢启》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　任穀城主簿。平仲登进士第，授洪州分宁县主簿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　任穀城主簿。三月，父延之与知桂州、兼经略安抚陆铣，提点刑狱公事余藻，兵马钤辖白均、徐印，新知郁林州姚原道，经略司勾当公事刘恕，会于广西伏波山还珠洞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1067')">1066-1067年</a>　任穀城主簿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年</a>　任穀城主簿。父延之作《邵州新迁州学记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　任穀城主簿。兄文仲用荐举台州军事推官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　任穀城主簿。七月庚子（十二日），荆湖北路转运使孔延之与判官吴太元不和，诏令江淮发运司及湖北提刑司礼量。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　任穀城主簿。兄文仲对策九千言，极言王安石新法之不当。王安石怒奏，上御批罢黜还故官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　任穀城主簿。父延之权开封府推官，前为湖北转运副使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　召任齐州教授。兄文仲以应制科策在京。四月，父延之以度支郎官知越州。<br /></div>

-----title
济南（历城）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a7bf5026896e445196fe3c2d8834f37d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a7bf5026896e445196fe3c2d8834f37d");'><span id='a7bf5026896e445196fe3c2d8834f37d_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年5月1日</a>　任齐州教授。父孔延之《会稽掇英总集》成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年7月23日</a>　任齐州教授。欧阳修卒，武仲作祭文。作品：代邵资政祭欧阳太师文。<div id='poem_1194210' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194210' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194210?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代邵资政祭欧阳太师文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1072年7月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194210")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194210_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194210'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194210'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194210_comment'></div>圣不世出，贤不世有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194210_comment'></div>繄公之生，与治为耦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194210_comment'></div>仁皇在位，公奋羁旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194210_comment'></div>声闻溢发，翔乎天衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194210_comment'></div>文章独行，后无辈匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194210_comment'></div>众星煌煌，孰较斗日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194210_comment'></div>初登侍从，进预宰司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194210_comment'></div>年四十间，亨塞险夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194210_comment'></div>坦不为机，独与道驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194210_comment'></div>皋、夔之言，载在简策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194210_comment'></div>周、召之烈，声于金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194210_comment'></div>脱屣重任，昔闻其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194210_comment'></div>公力方壮，联章乞身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194210_comment'></div>帝曰嗟咨，惟余旧臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194210_comment'></div>安车驷马，从容里第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194210_comment'></div>少休其勤，佥谓再起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194210_comment'></div>国之不幸，人也今亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194210_comment'></div>山颓玉折，间者陨伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194210_comment'></div>赠官太师，增赉后禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194210_comment'></div>哀荣则然，公去不复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194210_comment'></div>某之不肖，公遇优隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1194210_comment'></div>绪馀之及，其得则丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1194210_comment'></div>公在颍水，我官畿东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1194210_comment'></div>哭不为宾，窆不及视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1194210_comment'></div>终天之诀，此痛何已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1194210_comment'></div>不腆羞醪，致奠千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1194210_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1194210_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1194210_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年11月</a>　任齐州教授。十一月，父孔延之以“沮坏盐法”之名罢任越州，过杭赴京师，饮有美堂。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年11月</a>　任齐州教授。平仲有《寄常父》、《再用前意》诗寄武仲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年6月</a>　任齐州教授。武仲作祭文。作品：祭周茂叔文。<div id='poem_1194213' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194213' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194213?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭周茂叔文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1073年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194213")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194213_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194213'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194213'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194213_comment'></div>先君之壮，实难取友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194213_comment'></div>逢公豫章，握手驩厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194213_comment'></div>二十馀年，不知其久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194213_comment'></div>险夷之途，道义同守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194213_comment'></div>盖公之行，坦坦其诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194213_comment'></div>仁于鳏寡，信于友朋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194213_comment'></div>不戚于贫，志气内足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194213_comment'></div>不挠于势，廷争面触。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194213_comment'></div>施之吏治，或猛或宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194213_comment'></div>视俗张弛，民讴翕然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194213_comment'></div>既敏以明，学问又笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194213_comment'></div>纵横驰骤，瀚漫潴蓄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194213_comment'></div>先儒论撰，嵚崎诘曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194213_comment'></div>独纂圣微，浸酿醇熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194213_comment'></div>有书可传，万世之读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194213_comment'></div>惟愚不肖，幼也侍侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194213_comment'></div>公故怜之，以勉以饬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194213_comment'></div>称誉所长，以灌以植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194213_comment'></div>确如一朝，不见厌斁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194213_comment'></div>公之始终，明白纯备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194213_comment'></div>宜享遐年，显大当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1194213_comment'></div>如何不幸，缠疾艰踬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1194213_comment'></div>苦瘠日侵，遂以没地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1194213_comment'></div>报酢如此，孰晓天意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1194213_comment'></div>庐山之阴，松柏苍苍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1194213_comment'></div>归厝其丘，日吉晨良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1194213_comment'></div>悲号一诀，万世之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1194213_comment'></div>宁不我顾，有酒盈觞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1194213_comment'></div>追怀平生，曷日而忘。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194213_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年</a>　任齐州教授。夏，武仲与苏辙始交，有诗已佚。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
九江（德化）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2925d7f90c634e588ae56960be94a33f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2925d7f90c634e588ae56960be94a33f");'><span id='2925d7f90c634e588ae56960be94a33f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1078')">1073-1078年</a>，32-37岁</div><div id='2925d7f90c634e588ae56960be94a33f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年</a>　秋，武仲除江州推官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年</a>　任江州推官。二月，父延之卒，丁父忧。未几，母杨氏及祖母相继卒。武仲因丧二亲，毁疾特甚，右肱为之不举。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年7月</a>　任江州推官。将还江南,系舟于长芦之川，作文。作品：蝗说。<div id='poem_1194164' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194164' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194164?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蝗说</a><span class='authorDate'>（1074年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194164")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194164_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194164'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194164'>熙宁甲寅秋七月，予将还江南，系舟于长芦之川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194164_comment'></div>登高而望，见群飞而至者，若烟若澜，若大军之尘，自西而东，前后十馀里相属不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194164_comment'></div>野夫奔走相告曰：「蝗至矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194164_comment'></div>予曰：「蝗之来如何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194164_comment'></div>曰：「食我之田，齧我之桑，使我终岁无褐无粮」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194164_comment'></div>余曰：「嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194164_comment'></div>害无酷于此者矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194164_comment'></div>野夫哑然笑曰：「此非吾所谓害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194164_comment'></div>夫暝蝝之属，随阳而动，得雨而止，幸而岁丰时和，则其类泯焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194164_comment'></div>盖虽甚可畏恶，而其为祸犹有间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194164_comment'></div>以吾观之，今天下未尝有无蝗之岁，四方未尝有无蝗之国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194164_comment'></div>民之于利勤矣，罄其赀以裒种市牛，暴肩背，病手足，以趋田事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194164_comment'></div>及岁且成，则老幼相与计曰：是将穫之，以偿官之逋负也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194164_comment'></div>又曰：是将鬻之，以足官之赋泉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194164_comment'></div>凡数岁，矻矻而得之者，皆非吾有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194164_comment'></div>自祖及孙，岁被其患，而无有休期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194164_comment'></div>自燕至粤，其病一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194164_comment'></div>然则其为蝗也，大矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194164_comment'></div>今岁之蝗，不过遗种于一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194164_comment'></div>而每岁之蝗，流毒于天下，岂彼未之知耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194164_comment'></div>不然，宰相可以请，有司可以争矣，何其无闻耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194164_comment'></div>退因序其说。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1194164_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年9月26日</a>　在江州居父丧。九月乙酉葬父延之于江州之德化县仁贵龙泉原，以母杨氏祔。曾巩为延之作《中书舍人孔公墓志铭》。苏轼有《孔长源挽诗二首》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年</a>　在江州居父丧。黄庭坚有《次韵答常甫世弼》、《招子高二十二韵兼简常甫世弼》答武仲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　丁忧居家，是年服满。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>　兄文仲除充国子监直讲。弟平仲守秘书省著作郎充都水监勾当公事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>　任江州推官。有文。作品：秋赛诸庙文。<div id='poem_1194230' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194230' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194230?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋赛诸庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1077年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194230")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194230_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194230'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194230'>岁在丁巳，淮海一方，欲雨而雨，欲旸而旸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194230_comment'></div>和气浃充，岁以丰穰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194230_comment'></div>既溢于囷，既羡于场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194230_comment'></div>匪人之智，能赞阴阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194230_comment'></div>惟神之力，干之杳茫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194230_comment'></div>潜之无间，播之无疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194230_comment'></div>俾物蕃腴，无有坏伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194230_comment'></div>俾民佚乐，无近凶荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194230_comment'></div>惟古秋报，声于乐章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194230_comment'></div>功德之隆，畴其敢忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194230_comment'></div>挹酒于壶，登馔在堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194230_comment'></div>神其无恫，顾此馨香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194230_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1194230_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>　任江州推官，大病垂死，赖良医得活。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年</a>　任江州推官。三月，弟平仲以奉议郎通判虔州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年9月</a>　任江州推官。作文。作品：道士韦君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1194206' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194206' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194206?labeling=true' target='_blank'>道士卓君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰元年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1078年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194206")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194206_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194206'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194206'>卓君名玘，字玑石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194206_comment'></div>泉州晋江人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194206_comment'></div>弃家为道士，游四方，尝北济大河，南出岭表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194206_comment'></div>公卿大夫，多与相善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194206_comment'></div>成德军节度留后李璋奏得紫衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194206_comment'></div>吕诲自御史谪守江州，请君居天庆观，凡十八年乃退，属其事于弟子胡洞微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194206_comment'></div>元丰元年五月某日将逝，作三颂以遗所尝往来，大较皆落去世累，追逐神仙之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194206_comment'></div>享年七十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194206_comment'></div>以九月某日葬于德化县仁贵乡陵家垄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194206_comment'></div>君天资俊明，学问不倦，自道家书及星辰、五行、相术、壬遁之说，推考皆得其要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194206_comment'></div>与众人接，言若不能出口，及燕闲议论，援古證今，出入百家，听者为惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194206_comment'></div>明于事变，深沉有谋虑，未尝茍发，其所然否，人多不能损益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194206_comment'></div>天庆观久废不治，支扶败倾，以度岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194206_comment'></div>君身持俭约，下与厮役同食，斥其赢馀，以治新之，坛场殿室，皆用道家法仪，学者益盛，自君始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194206_comment'></div>及其卒也，闻者皆叹息，吊者皆哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194206_comment'></div>余早与君善，常奇君材而惜其不为世用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194206_comment'></div>及来过九江，适当君疾，叩门将见之，君方寝未寤，明日而君卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194206_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194206_comment'></div>死生之际，其迁徙迅速，盖未足道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194206_comment'></div>谓惟文字可以传于后，而致余所以厚君之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194206_comment'></div>乃为之铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1194206'>奄兮忽兮，其化以疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194206_comment'></div>生与没兮，若屈伸膝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1194206_comment'></div>君所自达，余又何悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1194206_comment'></div>其传则永，镵此铭兮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1194206_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
扬州（江都）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d0ac3de325294041a1478238885cd8b4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d0ac3de325294041a1478238885cd8b4");'><span id='d0ac3de325294041a1478238885cd8b4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1080')">1078-1080年</a>，37-39岁</div><div id='d0ac3de325294041a1478238885cd8b4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年</a>　罢江州推官任，改扬州州学教授。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年</a>　任扬州州学教授。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年</a>　任扬州州学教授。作文。作品：扬州芍药谱。<div id='poem_1194190' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194190' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194190?labeling=true' target='_blank'>扬州芍药谱</a><span class='authorDate'>（1080年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194190")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194190_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194190'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194190'>扬州芍药名于天下，非特以多为夸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194190_comment'></div>其敷腴盛大，而纤丽巧密，皆他州之所不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194190_comment'></div>至于名品相压，争妍斗奇，故者未厌，而新者已盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194190_comment'></div>州人相与惊异，交口称说，传于四方，名益以远，价益以重，与洛阳牡丹，俱贵于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194190_comment'></div>四方之人赍携金币来，市种以归者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194190_comment'></div>吾见其一岁而小变，三岁而大变，卒与常花无异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194190_comment'></div>由此，芍药之美，益专于扬州矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194190_comment'></div>负郭多旷土，种花之家，园舍相望，最盛于朱氏、丁氏、袁氏、徐氏、高氏、张氏，馀不可胜纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194190_comment'></div>畦分亩列，多者至数万根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194190_comment'></div>自三月初旬始开，浃旬而甚盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194190_comment'></div>游观者相属于路，幕帟相望，笙歌相闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194190_comment'></div>又浃旬，而衰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194190_comment'></div>大抵粗者先开，佳者后发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194190_comment'></div>高至尺馀，广至盈寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194190_comment'></div>其色以黄为最贵，所谓绯红千叶，乃其中下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194190_comment'></div>小人负携以卖，至于弃掷遗落，不甚爱惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194190_comment'></div>郑诗引芍药以明土风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194190_comment'></div>说者曰：香草也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194190_comment'></div>司马长卿《子虚赋》曰：「芍药之和，具而后御之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194190_comment'></div>说者曰：芍药根主和五藏，又辟毒气也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194190_comment'></div>谢宣城《直中书省诗》曰：「红药当阶翻」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194190_comment'></div>说者曰：草色红者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1194190_comment'></div>其义皆与今所谓芍药者合，但未有专言扬州者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1194190_comment'></div>唐之诗人，最以模写风物自喜，如庐仝、张祜之徒，皆居扬之日久，亦未有一语及之，是花品未有若今日之盛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1194190_comment'></div>余官于扬学，讲习之暇，尝载而之六氏之园，与凡佛宫道舍有佳花处，颇涉猎矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1194190_comment'></div>惧其久而遗忘也，闻之州人，得其粗，又属秀才满君方中、丁君时中，各集所闻，得其详，盖可纪者三十有三种。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1194190_comment'></div>世之有力者，或能邀致善工，列之图画，可揭而游四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1194190_comment'></div>然未若书之，可传于众也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1194190_comment'></div>乃具列其名，从而释之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1194190_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1194190'>御衣黄/<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>青苗黄楼子<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>/尹家二色黄楼子<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>/绛州紫苗楼子/<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>圆黄/<span class='inlineComment2'>（千叶而圆黄。）</span>硖石黄/<span class='inlineComment2'>（千叶而黄）</span>鲍家黄<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑸</sup>/石壕黄/<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑹</sup>寿州青苗黄楼子/<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑺</sup>黄丝头/<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑻</sup>道士黄/<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑼</sup>白缬子/<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑽</sup>金线冠子/<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑾</sup>金系腰/<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑿</sup>沔池红<span class='inlineComment2'>（千叶肉红）</span>/红缬子<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⒀</sup>/胡家缬<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⒁</sup>/玉楼子/<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⒂</sup>玉逍遥<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⒃</sup>/红楼子<span class='inlineComment2'>（千叶粉红）</span>/赤苗旋心<span class='inlineComment2'>（千叶深肉红。）</span>/青苗旋心<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⒄</sup>/二色红<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⒅</sup>/杨家花/<span class='inlineComment2'>（千叶粉红）</span>茅山紫楼子<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⒆</sup>/茅山冠子<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⒇</sup>/柳铺冠子/<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(21)</sup>软条冠子<span class='inlineComment2'>（千叶肉红）</span>/当州冠子<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(22)</sup>/多叶鞍子/<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(23)</sup>髻子<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(24)</sup>/红丝头/绯多叶。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1194190'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_0'>⑴ 千叶而淡黄，其香正如莲花，比他花色最殊绝。凡衣冠楼子、髻鞍，皆言其所似也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_3'>⑵ 叶小大间出。千馀层，或谓之千层阁。其苗青，故云尔。赤苗、紫苗仿此。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_5'>⑶ 与黄楼子不异，而间有微红。初出于尹氏，故名。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_6'>⑷ 初开时浅红，经数日乃黄，乃谓之红玉楼子。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_13'>⑸ 千叶而黄，大抵与红旋心相似，亦谓之黄旋心。但不甚高大，而又晚开。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_14'>⑹ 一丛之间，单叶、千叶往往兼有。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_16'>⑺ 与诸楼子相类，而花差小。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_18'>⑻ 其叶浅黄，大叶，中丛生细叶如丝也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_20'>⑼ 千叶而黄，最先开。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_22'>⑽ 花有结缬，而其外深红，经日则自缬之，外皆变为白也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_24'>⑾ 千叶浅红，间有细叶如金线。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_26'>⑿ 红叶中有晕。横绝如金带然。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_31'>⒀ 千叶，浅红，而叶端深红。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_33'>⒁ 千叶，肉红，而有缬文。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_34'>⒂ 千叶而白，上下叶中又出细叶数层。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_37'>⒃ 千叶而白，叶厚而大，如仙符也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_43'>⒄ 千叶肉红，花叶成旋。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_45'>⒅ 千叶淡红，而叶端深红。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_49'>⒆ 与诸楼子相似，而色紫。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_51'>⒇ 千叶而浅红，尤忌见日。自开至谢，常以幕覆，则色不烂。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_52'>(21) 千叶粉红，如柳叶，叠成冠子。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_57'>(22) 此花扬州素有之。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_58'>(23) 多叶粉红。其端或成双头，则谓之双头芍药，尤多开成鞍子，故谓之多叶鞍子。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194190_61'>(24) 其色紫红，下有大叶。其上细叶环抱，而黄叶杂出于其间。其香特甚。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1194190_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年</a>　任扬州州学教授。与苏辙唱和，苏辙有《次韵答孔武仲》诗。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
上饶
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4ca9b1c7b6f9483d8e45fa711011ba05_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4ca9b1c7b6f9483d8e45fa711011ba05");'><span id='4ca9b1c7b6f9483d8e45fa711011ba05_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1083')">1080-1083年</a>，39-42岁</div><div id='4ca9b1c7b6f9483d8e45fa711011ba05' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年</a>　任信州军事推官。编《南斋集稿》而序之。作品：南斋集稿序。<div id='poem_1194127' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194127' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194127?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南斋集藁序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1080年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194127")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194127_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194127'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194127'>元丰三年，余为信州从事，暇日，于南斋取旧所为文读之，忽而叹曰：「文章于学者之事末矣，昔之贤人，有达而在上者，其言甚简，而录于《尚书》，皋陶是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194127_comment'></div>有穷而在下者，其言甚简，而录于《论语》，颜渊是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194127_comment'></div>彼其粹美积于中，辉光发于外，一言出，四海传之以为师法，遂以不朽于无穷，岂区区自异于文墨耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194127_comment'></div>后世著书者，莫多于萧梁父子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194127_comment'></div>当其盛时，布于四方，盈衍竹帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194127_comment'></div>及其寖久，寖以零落，求一语之传不可得，卒与愚者均于没世而无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194127_comment'></div>然则文章岂可恃而久长哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194127_comment'></div>余自少喜为文辞，长游四方，从师交友，粗有所发，而才力卑弱不足以自振于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194127_comment'></div>中间患难侵陵，志气摧涸，俛仰之间，二十年矣，而为不增高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194127_comment'></div>夫以不可恃之文，而才之不足又如此，然吟口嗫嚅，老而不知止也，岂不惑哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194127_comment'></div>虽然，其志之所存，亦有见于此，不可废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194127_comment'></div>乃择其可观者，得议论、序记、颂赋、启状、祭文若干篇，古、律诗若干篇，录之以自览焉，命之曰《南斋集藁》。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1194127_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1081&endYear=1081')">1081年</a>　任信州军事推官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年5月</a>　任信州军事推官。五月，徐禧举武仲、邢恕为御史。五安礼、张璪议徐禧欲结附往时之人，欲以为党而罢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年6月25日</a>　任信州军事推官。作文。是年，兄文仲迁奉议郎，通判火山军。作品：信州新修广信门记。<div id='poem_1194177' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194177' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194177?labeling=true' target='_blank'>信州新修广信门记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1082年6月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194177")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194177_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194177'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194177'>信于江东为最远，介于闽、浙之间，宝货所出，号为富州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194177_comment'></div>其民勤于生业，而衣食赡足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194177_comment'></div>然地形狭隘，环以群山，带以长溪，而无高城深池捍御之固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194177_comment'></div>熙宁十年，诏天下郡县皆城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194177_comment'></div>朝奉郎虢略杨公适临是州，申戒官守，选兵属徒，吏士竞劝，以相厥事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194177_comment'></div>未几，周其三面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194177_comment'></div>而广信门者，城之南门也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194177_comment'></div>内直郡庾，适车马之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194177_comment'></div>外连长桥，控山川之险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194177_comment'></div>州之要冲，实在于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194177_comment'></div>然庳褊仄陋，几废而仅存，相因累年，恬不思革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194177_comment'></div>公命尽撤其旧，稍增大之，择材于山，发钱于库，令有素戒，人不告劳，凡旬有五日而成焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194177_comment'></div>重檐籥广翼而势严正，望之足以为壮丽，登之足以为高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194177_comment'></div>州人环观，悦喜呼舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194177_comment'></div>公以才行选为剧州，应物有馀，而持以厚重，事之细大，无不属心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194177_comment'></div>学敝则新之，驿敝则新之，库及仓敝则新之，市门敝则新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194177_comment'></div>至是，公治将成，归于朝廷，行有日矣，而夙夜精勤，严励如始至，不惮兴作，以惠于此邦之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194177_comment'></div>于是知公之为政，真有始终，而民之思公者，将至于无穷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194177_comment'></div>僚吏或愿使公之美久而益传，见属为文以刻于石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194177_comment'></div>元丰五年六月二十五日，军事推官孔某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1194177_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年12月</a>　任信州军事推官。作文。作品：信州祥符院新钟铭。<div id='poem_1194194' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194194' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194194?labeling=true' target='_blank'>信州祥符院新钟铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1082年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194194")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194194_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194194'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194194'>元丰五年十一月十三日，祥符院大钟成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194194_comment'></div>用铜三百钧有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194194_comment'></div>其高九尺有五寸，厚四寸，广六尺有三寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194194_comment'></div>主者僧晓儒，铸者诸杭张孝基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194194_comment'></div>越二十三日冬至击之，其声浑锽，震动城郭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194194_comment'></div>既浃旬，观者不休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194194_comment'></div>退则叹息，作生善意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194194_comment'></div>于是州将虢略杨亚甫为之铭，而其属孔武仲又铭于石以相之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194194_comment'></div>曰：上下无疆，旁暨八垠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194194_comment'></div>有告必闻，大声以震。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194194_comment'></div>叩之则应，不用则默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194194_comment'></div>既以时动，亦以时息。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1194194_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年</a>　任信州军事推官。作诗颂张夫人贤德。并邀苏辙作《同孔常父作张夫人诗》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年</a>　任信州军事推官。苏轼于东坡作草堂，武仲有诗。作品：苏子瞻雪堂。<div id='poem_58163' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58163' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58163?labeling=true' target='_blank'>苏子瞻雪堂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1082年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58163")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58163_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58163'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58163'>古县东边仄径开，先生曾此斸蒿莱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58163'>鸾凰一去应不返，花柳当年皆自栽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58163'>画壁苍茫留水墨，朱栏剥落长莓苔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58163'>邻翁笑我来何暮，检点风烟兴尽回。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58163'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58163_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年3月20日</a>　任信州军事推官。三月乙未，重建信州学成，武仲作记。作品：信州学记。<div id='poem_1194175' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194175' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194175?labeling=true' target='_blank'>信州学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年3月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194175")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194175_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194175'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194175'>信州新学，作于元丰五年十一月之庚寅，成于明年三月之乙未。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194175_comment'></div>既成，州之学者相与造余而言，请为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194175_comment'></div>惟圣宋刬五代之敝，合并四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194175_comment'></div>仁义礼乐之泽，洽于民心者，百有馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194175_comment'></div>而熙宁以来，学校最盛，内自京师，旁达边郡，聚士有舍，讲业有师，课试诵说与夫赏罚升黜之法，日增月长，以至大备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194175_comment'></div>四方之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194175_comment'></div>幸遇太平君子长养人材之时，裸粮束书，争集黉舍，惟恐在后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194175_comment'></div>信为江东之远州，南属闽，东被浙，士之待举者七百馀人，而例不除学官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194175_comment'></div>前此三年，天子从使者之请，以州官兼治学事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194175_comment'></div>余适为幕中吏，得以承乏庠序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194175_comment'></div>其地在子城之东，形势庳窄，民庐挟其旁，山林蔽其后，居处无夏屋，出入无高门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194175_comment'></div>而士之来者，犹相望不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194175_comment'></div>何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194175_comment'></div>彼相招以讲习论辨之益，而于居处之安则未暇议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194175_comment'></div>夫居不求其安者，士之分也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194175_comment'></div>上之所以待士者，岂当若此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194175_comment'></div>《传》曰：「处士就閒燕」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194175_comment'></div>盖教之不以其道，与居之不以其地，其病一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194175_comment'></div>有位者，孰不欲有为，以餍满人心之所愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194175_comment'></div>然文书有上下之禀，议论有同异之争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194175_comment'></div>或财局于府库而不可出，力隐于兵民而不可用，此事之所以常废，而人不被其泽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194175_comment'></div>窃为学者忧之，会转运判官郏公亶知州事，杨公仲孺相与谋议，以招学者为先急，乃发库钱五十万以付有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1194175_comment'></div>而余实与二三联事之人，升降险阻，拟度广输。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1194175_comment'></div>凡地之在民者，劝以贸易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1194175_comment'></div>良材坚甓，出于诸县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1194175_comment'></div>然后隳山发石，剪斸草木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1194175_comment'></div>高者损以为平，狭者培以为广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1194175_comment'></div>旁积步道以属于旧学之北，而营其上为经史之阁，教授之堂，诸生之舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1194175_comment'></div>环起参出，整若棋局，视旧之广加倍，以增高丈有三尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1194175_comment'></div>诸山森然，若翔若踊，出于三面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1194175_comment'></div>使士之来者去湫底而即亢爽，脱卑闇而登高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1194175_comment'></div>又为之大其正门，高其墙垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1194175_comment'></div>庖湢之所皆易新之，而饮食燕息之具滋设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1194175_comment'></div>此余与二三僚所以佐公上之命，而劝相学者之万一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1194175_comment'></div>夫学之道，先后有伦，始卒有渐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1194175_comment'></div>不得其端，虽强力不可以至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1194175_comment'></div>至孟子曰：「学则三代共之，皆所以明人伦也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1194175_comment'></div>夫所谓人伦者，岂他乎哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1194175_comment'></div>其分见于君臣父子之间，其守寓于仁义忠信之际，其文礼乐诗书，其声籥鼓琴瑟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1194175_comment'></div>士之志于道者，不惮岁月以游心于其间，至于四十年焉，则可以仕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1194175_comment'></div>此圣人所谓不惑之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1194175_comment'></div>廓之益广，浚之益深，又十年焉，则性命之理较然于前，若数一二，则可以为大夫矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1194175_comment'></div>此圣人所谓知天命之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1194175_comment'></div>然则知天命，当在四十之后，而学之所教者，未成材之士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1194175_comment'></div>古之人知此而求之，是以行应规矩，智揆万变，处焉可以为子弟师法，出焉足以有功烈于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1194175_comment'></div>盖道德在己，则其成物为不难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1194175_comment'></div>今学者既得朋友以相与处矣，则学之序可以不知哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1194175_comment'></div>按旧学作于嘉祐七年，距今未远，而栋梁有败折者，甓瓦有断缺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1194175_comment'></div>物之兴坏不可久，其势如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1194175_comment'></div>后数十年间，则今日之新，岂特为故耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1194175_comment'></div>意必有更而大之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1194175_comment'></div>不为之记，则惧无以知今所以兴作之详也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1194175_comment'></div>乃为之书，使来者稽焉。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_1194175'></div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1194175_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
湘潭
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年6月</a>　任宣德郎、差知潭州湘潭县事。是月，弟平仲覃恩转朝奉郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年6月</a>　除宣德郎、差知潭州湘潭县事。夏，兄文仲覃恩转承议郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　任宣德郎、差知潭州湘潭县事。作文。作品：焚黄疏。兴国僧房诗序。<div id='poem_1194232' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194232' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194232?labeling=true' target='_blank'>焚黄疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1084年6月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194232")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194232_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194232'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194232'>元丰七年六月二十九日，宣德郎、新差知潭州湘潭县事孔武仲，谨告于先考中散、先妣太君杨氏之坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194232_comment'></div>吾家不幸，怙恃相继丧亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194232_comment'></div>其后诸孤，散仕四方，靡有定处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194232_comment'></div>又十一年，而后文仲、平仲并官于朝，赖天子仁圣，以孝治天下，许以子恩推及父母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194232_comment'></div>粤今四月，得告赠先考中散大夫，先妣德化县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194232_comment'></div>已附递往火山军文仲收掌供养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194232_comment'></div>外有录黄二轴，谨因武仲南归，焚献于坟下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194232_comment'></div>魂而有灵，膺受多福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194232_comment'></div>武仲无任涕泣追慕之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194232_comment'></div>谨告。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1194232_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1194123' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194123' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194123?labeling=true' target='_blank'>兴国僧房诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1084年7月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194123")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194123_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194123'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194123'>主上稽六典，修废官，大治新省于西华门外，丞相以下日入焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194123_comment'></div>于是辟兴国寺之北门，以通车马之道，与省门咫尺相望，而朝士大夫受事于尚书者，皆集于兴国矣，税屋之赀，为之翔踊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194123_comment'></div>主僧争饰其庐，以要四方之宾客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194123_comment'></div>其深邃清洁，莫如西法华胜公之房，余幸而得居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194123_comment'></div>胜公，郓人，性方严，笃于斋戒，善讲经论，与余非故人，而特相好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194123_comment'></div>是时联舍而居者，开封竹元珍，湛静好学，虽在逆旅，而所携书亦数百卷，闭门不治往来，日夜诵说，有绳墨尺度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194123_comment'></div>余得二人者与之处，谈笑融怡，足以引日而忘其为客之久也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194123_comment'></div>于閒暇时，作为歌诗以自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194123_comment'></div>自二月至于五月，得三十八篇，录于左方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194123_comment'></div>而受牒吏部，得县为湖南，繇所馆晨出南薰门，以望九江，道途所得，又三十五篇，亦附于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194123_comment'></div>昔周人为《采薇》之歌曰：「昔我往矣，杨柳依依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194123_comment'></div>今我来思，雨雪霏霏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194123_comment'></div>盖伤行役之勤，感时物之变也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194123_comment'></div>余之是行也，冒大寒，历暑潦，凡半岁而后得止鞍马之劳，筋骸之惫，殆无馀力矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194123_comment'></div>其感于物，动于心，发于言，不为讥嘲以忤群众，从容自道而已，亦诗人之志也欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194123_comment'></div>元丰七年七月五日某谨序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1194123_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年8月16日</a>　任宣德郎、差知潭州湘潭县事。七月二十八日，张公美卒，武仲哭之。八月十六日，作文。作品：张公美偈言记。<div id='poem_1194180' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194180' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194180?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张公美偈言记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1084年8月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194180")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194180_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194180'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194180'>左藏库副使张宗旦，字公美，开封人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194180_comment'></div>元丰七年七月二十八日卒于江州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194180_comment'></div>前卒之两月，以书告诀于亲识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194180_comment'></div>病且革，群僧以诵佛为请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194180_comment'></div>公美颔之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194180_comment'></div>遽问之曰：「何谓自在」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194180_comment'></div>皆唯莫对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194180_comment'></div>公美大书三十二字以示之，曰：「法本心生，心因法昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194180_comment'></div>有觉于此者，名自在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194180_comment'></div>自在真空，顿然明彻，去住寻常，晓云春雪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194180_comment'></div>已目瞑，复寤曰：「吾意若未释然者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194180_comment'></div>改其卒句曰：「春风晓雪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194180_comment'></div>投笔而绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194180_comment'></div>明日，余入哭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194180_comment'></div>视其遗草，皆公美手书也，而辞句洒然，无世俗气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194180_comment'></div>问其子沔曰：「公美尝学佛乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194180_comment'></div>曰：「往年尝诵金刚经之四句，曰：『一切有为法，如梦幻泡影，如露亦如电，应作如是观』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194180_comment'></div>家人怪而止之，遂不复言，今四十年矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194180_comment'></div>呜呼，亦异矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194180_comment'></div>公美者，盖内有所得，而不资于学问者与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194180_comment'></div>昔公美为扬州都巡检使，余为州学教授，数相往来，实不见其一语及佛书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194180_comment'></div>其宽厚谨默，不臧否人物，宜能藏其所得，不衒于世俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1194180_comment'></div>则今日之发，岂偶然哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1194180_comment'></div>世之处山林，诵释老者，平居之日，饰行而高言，若不可望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1194180_comment'></div>然死生之变，或不能自达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1194180_comment'></div>而公美属纩之际，神识不乱，视去其形骸而游太空，若由东乡适西里；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1194180_comment'></div>顾其妻孥号于卧侧，如旅人相遇于市而将散也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1194180_comment'></div>视其四体托于枕席，如浮云堕叶役然而止其旁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1194180_comment'></div>不如是，安能出至言乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1194180_comment'></div>公美既卒，九江之人皆能道其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1194180_comment'></div>僧遵邈欲其传于久也，将刻于石，属余言其本末，故为之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1194180_comment'></div>八月十六日，鲁国孔某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1194180_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　任宣德郎、差知潭州湘潭县事。是年张耒赴官咸平往淮南。武仲有诗。作品：送张文潜之淮南。<div id='poem_58439' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58439' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58439?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送张文潜之淮南</a><span class='authorDate'>（1084年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58439")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58439_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58439'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58439'>瀛馆登仙俊，金闺引籍优。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58439_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58439'>辞班见天子，行色动诸侯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58439_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58439'>楚日篮舆暖，淮南画舸遒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58439_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58439'>归时春已好，迟子曲江头。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58439_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58439'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58439_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　任宣德郎、差知潭州湘潭县事。与钱协、苏轼等唱和。作品：钱穆仲有高丽松扇馆中多得者以诗求之。<span class='inlineComment2'>（吴洪泽等《宋人年谱丛刊》第五册；李春梅《三孔事迹编年》第二八九五页：“按：据《长编》卷三三九，是年钱协出使高丽，带回高丽松扇分赠同僚，众人作诗咏之。苏轼有《和张耒高丽松扇》。）</span>内阁钱公宠惠高丽扇以梅州大纸报之仍赋诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（吴洪泽等《宋人年谱丛刊》第五册；李春梅《三孔事迹编年》第二八九五页：“按：据《长编》卷三三九，是年钱协出使高丽，带回高丽松扇分赠同僚，众人作诗咏之。苏轼有《和张耒高丽松扇》。）</span><div id='poem_58464' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58464' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58464?labeling=true' target='_blank'>钱穆仲有高丽松扇馆中多得者以诗求之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1084年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58464")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_58464_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58464'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58464'>巨鳌昂头鲸掉尾，东顾沧溟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>天接水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58464'>钱公涉险如通渠，破帆<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：一作扁舟）</span>一抹三千里。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58464'>岛夷之国远且偏，归来逢人语辄喜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58464'>大荒茫茫最宜松，直从旷野连深宫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58464'>听声卧影已不俗，况作团扇摇清风<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_58464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_58464'>人情重远由来事，不贵黄金贵楛矢。<div id='poem_sentence_5_58464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_58464'>况有新诗传四方，群豪追随弄荐章。<div id='poem_sentence_6_58464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_58464'>我虽相见无所得，坐忆松鹤生微凉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_58464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_58464'>钱公治迹压张赵，偷儿破胆皆摧藏。<div id='poem_sentence_8_58464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_58464'>桴鼓不鸣已三月，凛凛霜威破残热。<div id='poem_sentence_9_58464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_58464'>从公觅扇更觅诗，愿报琼瑶无已时。<div id='poem_sentence_10_58464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_58464'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_58464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_58464'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_58464_0'>⑴ 原校：百家作溟茫</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_58464_0'>⑵ 原校：一云国人裁治多纤巧，故有团扇饶清风</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_58464_0'>⑶ 自注：往年在庐山，见僧房有高丽松扇，敛之不盈寸，舒之则雪山松鹤，意趣甚远。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_58464_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_58355' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58355' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58355?labeling=true' target='_blank'>内閤钱公宠惠高丽扇以梅州大纸报之仍赋诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1084年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58355")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_58355_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58355'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58355'>昨夜秋风来户庭，残灯闪灭微凉生。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58355'>得公团扇未及用，挂向空堂神骨清。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58355'>但将远趣醒耳目，不独暑月排歊蒸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58355'>惭当厚意无以报，前诗空说玖与琼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58355'>漆箱犹有南中纸，阔似棋枰净如水。<div id='poem_sentence_4_58355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_58355'>传闻造之自梅州，蛮奴赤脚踏溪流。<div id='poem_sentence_5_58355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_58355'>银波渗彻云蟾髓，入轴万杵光欲浮。<div id='poem_sentence_6_58355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_58355'>收藏终恐非吾物，宝剑银钩有时失。<div id='poem_sentence_7_58355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_58355'>不如包卷归文房，钱公家世能文章。<div id='poem_sentence_8_58355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_58355'>五日京兆聊尔耳，归步金銮上<span class='inlineComment2'>（豫章本作登）</span>玉堂。<div id='poem_sentence_9_58355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_58355'>玉堂不复知吏事，紫橐华簪<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：一作荷囊）</span>奉天子。<div id='poem_sentence_10_58355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_58355'>凤阁曾观思涌泉，谪仙今振辞如绮。<div id='poem_sentence_11_58355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_58355'>不似冷官太苦辛，吟哦风月愁山鬼。<div id='poem_sentence_12_58355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_58355'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_58355_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年1月</a>　任宣德郎、差知潭州湘潭县事。作文。作品：仁和县君许氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1194204' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194204' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194204?labeling=true' target='_blank'>仁和县君许氏墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰八年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194204")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194204_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194204'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194204'>夫人姓许氏，衡州衡阳人，处士永宗之女，朝议大夫黄公之妻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194204_comment'></div>黄氏于衡阳为大族，朝议于时为名臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194204_comment'></div>夫人年十有八归黄氏，事舅姑为贤妇，佐其夫为贤妻，有子为贤母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194204_comment'></div>朝议公立身以道，时列王廷，出守方郡，在进思退，燕休于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194204_comment'></div>夫人与之齐，凡五十有八年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194204_comment'></div>年七十有六，元丰七年十月二十一日，卒于第舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194204_comment'></div>自始封至卒，凡四受县，始于金堂，终于仁和云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194204_comment'></div>明年正月五日，葬于东郊某原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194204_comment'></div>夫人幼而令淑，慎静寡言，不遽白人是非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194204_comment'></div>自奉养甚约，而赒施无所顾惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194204_comment'></div>奉佛尤专。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194204_comment'></div>平居未尝有疾，比老，起居饮食如少时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194204_comment'></div>其将终也，具肴酒，合亲属，从容语诀，附以家事，踰二日而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194204_comment'></div>子男二人：长曰钧，忠正军节度推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194204_comment'></div>次曰锜，全州司理参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194204_comment'></div>女三人：长早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194204_comment'></div>次适耒阳主簿孙钦臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194204_comment'></div>次适衡阳进士狄光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194204_comment'></div>孙四人：长曰端，权知韶州翁源县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194204_comment'></div>次曰竦，潭州湘乡县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194204_comment'></div>次尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194204_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1194204_comment'></div>夫人之志行与其福禄，终始之盛，充足完合，皆无憾者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1194204_comment'></div>惟其传于后故不朽，载于文为无穷，宜有可信之言，刻于金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1194204_comment'></div>此其子若孙勤勤以属余，使为铭者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1194204_comment'></div>乃为掇其大要，而书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1194204_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1194204'>女德伊何，惟顺之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1194204_comment'></div>妇德非他，夫子之随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1194204_comment'></div>夫人之修，匪跋匪激。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1194204_comment'></div>循其分守，以有成德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1194204_comment'></div>人归以誉，天锡以年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1194204_comment'></div>噫嗟夫人，福禄之全。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1194204_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年10月</a>　任宣德郎、差知潭州湘潭县事。十月，兄文仲自承议郎迁校书郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年9月</a>　任宣德郎、差知潭州湘潭县事。作文。作品：吴氏夫人墓志铭。<div id='poem_1194205' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194205' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194205?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴氏夫人墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰八年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194205")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194205_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194205'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194205'>夫人姓吴氏，世家于抚州金溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194205_comment'></div>赠尚书屯田员外郎德筠之曾孙，都官员外郎敏之孙，虔州信丰令蒙之女，淮南节度使推官、知信州上饶县事李君介夫之继室也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194205_comment'></div>二十三而归，五十而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194205_comment'></div>卒之明年，当元丰八年九月初五日而葬，其子侁、仿以书属余为铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194205_comment'></div>昔夫人之子份，笃学而早世，余实铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194205_comment'></div>间未再岁，又铭夫人之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194205_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194205_comment'></div>康宁寿考，世之所谓福者，付与于人，无有匮竭，而造物者啬之，何耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194205_comment'></div>以夫人之积德累行，而报施如此其薄！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194205_comment'></div>所谓命者不可知，而为善未必祥耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194205_comment'></div>此余之所欲载而使后世知之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194205_comment'></div>夫人以孝事其舅姑，以礼相其君子，其训诸子以义，其接婢妾以仁，其事上不以劳故懈，其居丧不以久故易，其念父母不以壮老故衰，其恤幼孤不以非己生故薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194205_comment'></div>李氏家世贵显，亲属逾百口，无内外长幼卑尊之人，皆推以为贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194205_comment'></div>而李君亦曰：「吾縻于小官，邅迍蹇塞之日久，而心能安之者，吴氏助我也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194205_comment'></div>夫人之大母曾氏，谏议大夫致尧之女，博学善持论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194205_comment'></div>夫人少习见之，故于文字多所通解，尤喜读佛书及唐人歌诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194205_comment'></div>有子份、侁、仔、效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194205_comment'></div>份及仔早卒，馀皆应进士举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194205_comment'></div>女一人，嫁进土叶观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194205_comment'></div>夫人墓在金溪归德乡之株塘原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194205_comment'></div>其卒在上饶官舍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194205_comment'></div>以元丰七年九月十四日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1194205_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1194205'>李氏寓洪，蔼蔚蕃昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1194205_comment'></div>至于妇族，必邦之良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1194205_comment'></div>夫人家抚，族良且大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1194205_comment'></div>既得所从，协相于内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1194205_comment'></div>善积有馀，顾不足年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1194205_comment'></div>夫方壮强，妇弃而先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1194205_comment'></div>归葬株塘，松柏始植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1194205_comment'></div>幼长于斯，今又安宅。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1194205_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年12月13日</a>　任宣德郎、差知潭州湘潭县事。作文。是月，孔武仲自奉议郎除秘书省正字。作品：刘氏家传跋尾。<div id='poem_1194139' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194139' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194139?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刘氏家传跋尾</a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年12月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194139")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194139_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194139'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194139'>元丰八年冬，某以职事见河南刘公于长沙，得与读家传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194139_comment'></div>自北齐至于本朝，十更国姓，而刘氏衣冠不绝，忠臣义士，文学之老，世有其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194139_comment'></div>公兄伯寿，年逾七十，精明如少壮时，爵列三品，而身游方外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194139_comment'></div>公以行学政事见器人主，跻方面，期年政成，且乘驿归奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194139_comment'></div>兄弟进退虽不同，皆为士大夫所推仰，又一时之盛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194139_comment'></div>尝观春秋之世，区区晋楚，分国一隅，下至宋、鲁、郑地，不过百里，其卿大夫之贵且富，往往与其国盛衰相上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194139_comment'></div>今刘氏积德如此，子孙贤才，衣冠世袭之盛，其将与宋无穷乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194139_comment'></div>十二月十三日孔某题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1194139_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年12月</a>　自奉议郎除秘书省正字。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年</a>　任宣德郎、差知潭州湘潭县事。作文。作品：徐成之园亭三咏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（该诗作于湘潭令任上。）</span><div id='poem_58457' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58457' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58457?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徐成之园亭三咏<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>竹径桃花</a><span "poem_title_58457")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58457_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58457'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58457'>辟地不盈亩，点缀成阻修。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58457'>相招竹林逸，更作桃源游。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58457'>绰约新饮露，琅玕曾倚秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58457'>春风荡人意，此境独清幽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58457'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58457_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58240' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58240' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58240?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58240'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58240'>异国携来看愈新，移当樽俎会嘉宾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58240_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58240'>虽无绝艳惊流俗，为有清香得近人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58240_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58240'>烛下更宜观态度，酒阑尤觉醒精神。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58240_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58240'>湖南莫作淹留叹，已见浔阳二月春。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58240_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58240'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58240_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58456' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58456' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58456?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>石盘</a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_58456_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58456'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58456'>攻玉为方盘，可据以饮食。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58456'>又可安文枰<span class='inlineComment2'>（豫章本作楸）</span>，两仙相对奕。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58456'>簿书应接罢，胥不留踪迹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58456'>散步到其间，如临苍山壁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58456'>下有清冷波，滟滟欲侵席。<div id='poem_sentence_4_58456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_58456'>坐兼仁智乐，岂独烦襟释。<div id='poem_sentence_5_58456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年</a>　任宣德郎、差知潭州湘潭县事。作诗。作品：石盘。<span class='inlineComment2'>（该诗作于湘潭令任上。）</span>祠二庙之明日未得顺风呈同行。<span class='inlineComment2'>（该诗作于湘潭令任上。）</span>庙下候风呈同行。<span class='inlineComment2'>（该诗作于湘潭令任上。）</span>登君山二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（该诗作于湘潭令任上。）</span>湘潭二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（该诗作于湘潭令任上。）</span>自君山还岳阳。<span class='inlineComment2'>（该诗作于湘潭令任上。）</span><div id='poem_58456' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58456' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58429?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祠二庙之明日未得顺风呈同行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58429")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_58429_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58429'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58429'>岳州西祠从古有，控带洞庭湖之口。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58429'>前对隐显明灭之湘山，下接渊沦汹涌之长川。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58429'>茫茫白沙连绝屿，淡淡古木蟠苍烟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58429'>昭灵王，左安流，右翠帐，朱幡拥前后。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58429'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_58429", 58429, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>锯牙</span>虎视森两厢，气骨生狞欲奔走。<div id='poem_sentence_4_58429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_58429'>我来缆舟日已昏，袍靴跪听祠官言。<div id='poem_sentence_5_58429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_58429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_58429'>焚香奏酒殊无计，伏渚藏汀姑有待。<div id='poem_sentence_8_58429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_58429'>二王威神世所传，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_58429", 58429, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>钤摄</span>鬼怪宾灵仙。<div id='poem_sentence_9_58429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_58429'>好风相送势不难，舒卷造化须臾间。<div id='poem_sentence_10_58429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_58429_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58414' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58414' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58414?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庙下候风呈同行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58414")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_58414_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58414'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58414'>楚水千百源，洞庭为壮观。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58414'>势居七泽右，地裂荆吴半。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58414'>而我泛扁舟<span class='inlineComment2'>（豫章本作舟归）</span>，飘然一归<span class='inlineComment2'>（豫章本作孤）</span>雁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58414'>来之岂为益，去亦未<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_58414", 58414, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>足算</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58414'>胡不吹清波，纵发如飞翰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_58414'>朝辞庙山曲，午泊巴陵岸。<div id='poem_sentence_5_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_58414'>况有三面风，迎送俱无间。<div id='poem_sentence_6_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_58414'>定非偏薄厚，以掇行旅讪。<div id='poem_sentence_7_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_58414'>奈何苦流滞，兀兀晨复旰。<div id='poem_sentence_8_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_58414'>采芹朝当蔬，伐竹暮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_58414", 58414, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>供爨</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_58414'>舟师三十人，饿虎奔刍豢。<div id='poem_sentence_10_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_58414'>使之裹粮绝，虑有探囊患。<div id='poem_sentence_11_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_58414'>二王东南望，貌像颇辉焕。<div id='poem_sentence_12_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_58414'>歌鼓岁无休，香灯夜侵旦。<div id='poem_sentence_13_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_58414'>我为江湖士，乞灵从弱冠。<div id='poem_sentence_14_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_58414'>四到祠宫下，霜髯今已灿。<div id='poem_sentence_15_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_58414'>王其故旧恤，勿以涂人看。<div id='poem_sentence_16_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_58414'>尊师况慈忍<span class='inlineComment2'>（豫章本作悲）</span>，善道阴有赞。<div id='poem_sentence_17_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_58414'>王心或未回，师颊固宜缓。<div id='poem_sentence_18_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_58414'>灵<span class='inlineComment2'>（豫章本作杯）</span>珓似见许，归来整樯幔。<div id='poem_sentence_19_58414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_58414'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_58414_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58504' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58504' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58504?labeling=true'
