id='poem_content_58504'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58504'>径欲涉方壶，沧溟何太远。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58504'>试登君山杪，直望苍梧晚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58504'>寂无纤尘动，迥快千里眼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58504'>胜境真少伦，仙山连禁苑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58504'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58504_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58503' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58503' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58503?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_58503_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58503'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58503'>楚水吞东南，皤然天一腹。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58503'>君山枕波面，半插蛾眉绿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58503'>平空接游气，杳荡无川陆。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58503'>归桨恨匆匆，残阳挂乔木。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58503'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58503_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58291' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58291' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58291?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湘潭二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58291")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58291_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58291'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58291'>禄仕飘然寄楚乡，才能苦短志方强。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58291'>已栽绿柳如彭泽，况有黄金似栎阳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58291'>风飐湘波天影动，云来衡岳雨声长。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58291'>尚疑卑湿难安处，更起西边百尺堂<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58291'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_58291'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_58291_0'>⑴ 自注：湘潭近有告发金坑者。余作堂于厅西，谓之月堂。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_58291_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_58500' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58500' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58500?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58500_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58500'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58500'>县街重复俯惊湍，正与湘江咫尺间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58500_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58500'>侵齧最忧东汇水，蔽遮惟有北来山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58500_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58500'>清流倒影楼台壮，白瓦连云市井间。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58500_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58500'>捍患持危功不小，亭亭千古镇荒湾<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58500_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58500'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58500_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_58500'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_58500_0'>⑴ 自注：县西七里有唐兴山，耸出江上，水趋南岸，故邑居得完。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_58500_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_58137' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58137' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58137?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自君山还岳阳</a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58137")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58137_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58137'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58137'>云山深处望潇湘，岩石<span class='inlineComment2'>（豫章本作谷）</span>沈沈已夕阳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58137'>却整舟帆<span class='inlineComment2'>（豫章本作航）</span>凌浩渺，回看城郭似家乡。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58137'>挥戈径欲回羲驭，散发今知出吕梁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58137'>不是浮休动归兴，对眠犹可借禅床<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58137'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_58137'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_58137_0'>⑴ 自注：是日浮休居士张芸老欲速归，遂乘晚北渡。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_58137_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年</a>　任宣德郎、差知潭州湘潭县事。作文。作品：碧湘湖录。<span class='inlineComment2'>（该文作于湘潭令任上。）</span>记言。<span class='inlineComment2'>（该文作于湘潭令任上。）</span>故陇西李君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1194186' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194186' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194186?labeling=true' target='_blank'>碧湘湖录</a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194186")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194186_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194186'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194186'>长沙有碧湘湖者，自马氏始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194186_comment'></div>僧惠严，吴人，自杭州来依马武穆王，武穆重之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194186_comment'></div>一日思归，武穆曰：「公忆西湖耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194186_comment'></div>乃为置寺湖西，有辟湖于寺外，旁引群山，下通湘水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194186_comment'></div>其后惠严卒于寺，至今堂中有真身存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194186_comment'></div>马氏乘唐之乱，窃有一方，恃其兵力，北斗高氏，南盗岭表，遂为强国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194186_comment'></div>武穆始称王，卒，传子希声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194186_comment'></div>希声卒，弟希范立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194186_comment'></div>希范卒，弟希广立，而湖南乱矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194186_comment'></div>希范最为奢侈，事土木，作会春园兴诸佛庙，增赋于民，上下彫困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194186_comment'></div>是时，牙将丁思勤力谏不从，遂自杀，其无道如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194186_comment'></div>独武穆守节俭，号为长者，待士有礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194186_comment'></div>然绝山障水，以奉一浮屠，亦过甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194186_comment'></div>其父子之所为，岂相远哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194186_comment'></div>然至今为湖西之异观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194186_comment'></div>余至真身寺，遂游湘上，憩乔木之阴，观鱼鸟之乐，日暮忘归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194186_comment'></div>感马氏之兴废，而慨然于怀也，因录其本末云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1194186_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1194187' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194187' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194187?labeling=true' target='_blank'>记言</a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194187")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194187_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194187'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194187'>孔氏子居浔阳城中，怠于应接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194187_comment'></div>乃以二丁夫肩舆，上田家坡，历宝严精舍，而至于龙泉之源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194187_comment'></div>秋阳虽壮，西风已厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194187_comment'></div>松竹之间，索索然颓檐败砌，脱叶相触。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194187_comment'></div>新雨过，泉水潺潺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194187_comment'></div>稻之未刈者，僵于亩上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194187_comment'></div>清在泉间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194187_comment'></div>予怠而休，息而作，扶藜杖，曳芒履，登蹑高原，路微如线，随佶曲而往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194187_comment'></div>顾瞻两钟，迥望庐阜，风景萧瑟，心旷爽而体逍遥，若有忘世遗俗，栖身山谷之意，而未决者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194187_comment'></div>乃以杖击梧桐之枝而歌曰：「松风之飕飕兮，可以散吾之忧兮！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194187_comment'></div>泉声之溅溅兮，可以荡吾之烦兮！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194187_comment'></div>驱驰四方今有年兮，追世奉俗礼节繁兮，不如此居仰听风、俯听泉兮」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194187_comment'></div>又歌曰：「登彼高丘，顾瞻山川兮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194187_comment'></div>草茂土旷，人舒闲兮！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194187_comment'></div>场圃阴阴，时果繁兮！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194187_comment'></div>湓城之东，吾故园兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194187_comment'></div>舍之不得已，归亦适然兮」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194187_comment'></div>方其歌也，气正色怡，声如凤凰，绕乎丛谷之间，闻乎数里之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194187_comment'></div>有一老叟，庞眉皓首，出乎林间，而揖余曰：「良苦，余不与世接久矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194187_comment'></div>以子之容，似有道者，故来与子言，将以质子之志焉，抑子有帷幄沉深之虑乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194187_comment'></div>曰：「无」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194187_comment'></div>「有边陲金革之忧乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1194187_comment'></div>曰：「无」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1194187_comment'></div>子之名不挂于士师之籍乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1194187_comment'></div>曰：「我无罪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1194187_comment'></div>「子之勋不铭于司常之旂乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1194187_comment'></div>曰：「我无功」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1194187_comment'></div>「入不肩随公卿，出不身先士卒，子之责轻矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1194187_comment'></div>内有厌俗之意，外有无责之身，知山林乐如此，徘徊而不即者，吾不知其说也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1194187_comment'></div>曰：「叟论甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1194187_comment'></div>吾将与妇计之，次与吾儿计之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1194187_comment'></div>叟哑然笑曰：「已矣，子之诈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1194187_comment'></div>昔列子居郑，貌有饥色，国相遗之粟而不受，其妻拊心曰：『妾闻为有道者之妻子，皆得逸乐，今有饥色，君过而遗先生食不受，岂非命耶』！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1194187_comment'></div>列子不听也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1194187_comment'></div>善处身者盖如此，岂决策于儿女辈哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1194187_comment'></div>曰：「吾之道未及列子，而欲当其任耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1194187_comment'></div>是犹以六尺童子负千钧之重，绝肩折胫，而途不加进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1194187_comment'></div>岂若量力而为之之逸哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1194187_comment'></div>且衣不被体，廉士蹙眉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1194187_comment'></div>食不充肠，勇夫沮气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1194187_comment'></div>以此治人，旬日犹所难合，况与之终身处者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1194187_comment'></div>子休矣，讫将从子游，姑少俟我」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1194187_comment'></div>叟默而喜，顾而叹，踰岭而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1194187_comment'></div>不知其名氏<span class='inlineComment2'>（《宗伯集》卷一六。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1194187_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_1194187'>清在泉间：库本作「果在树间」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1194187_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1194207' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194207' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194207?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故陇西李君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194207")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194207_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194207'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194207'>君姓李氏，讳份，字文淑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194207_comment'></div>洪州新建人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194207_comment'></div>李氏世为江南大家，其贵者，列侍从，以为卿为郎，皆有显闻于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194207_comment'></div>其外亲旁属，累至公相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194207_comment'></div>家藏书万卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194207_comment'></div>君兄弟若干人皆进于学，或由乡举登进士第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194207_comment'></div>君为人静专，而刻苦自励，凡六经、诸子之说，穷昼夜讲求，非食与寝，书未尝去手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194207_comment'></div>滑稽慢戏之言，纷华盛丽之好，不出于口，不接于耳目，人谓君必将有盛德以大其宗门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194207_comment'></div>年二十，以疾卒于江州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194207_comment'></div>又期年，而其父几甫官信州，数与余往来，道君之平生，未尝不咨嗟叹息，继以泣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194207_comment'></div>且曰：「吾儿生无以见于世，庶几有闻于后也，为我铭之，以信于无穷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194207_comment'></div>余譬解之曰：「士生于世，虽有聪明敏捷之才，而教或不尽其方，学或不竭其力，或中道而止以忘其素习，或见利趋逐以溺于其心，此朋友之过，而父兄之恨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194207_comment'></div>今文淑皆异于是，惟其年之不长，不得成其志耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194207_comment'></div>此知义理者之所能平，虽圣人犹不怨也，子又何悲焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194207_comment'></div>虽然，余不可以不铭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194207_comment'></div>君卒于元丰五年五月某甲子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194207_comment'></div>以某年某日某甲子葬于某县某乡某里某原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194207_comment'></div>世系有先侍郎尚书之碑，金部司农之铭，此不著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194207_comment'></div>著其不幸短命而死者，以慰其亲云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194207_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1194207'>苗而不秀者有矣，夫君其是已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194207_comment'></div>士亡良朋，父失贤子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1194207_comment'></div>西山峨峨，播以章水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1194207_comment'></div>其生勤劳，归息于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1194207_comment'></div>呜呼，其已矣夫！</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1194207'></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1194207_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年2月</a>　任宣德郎、差知潭州湘潭县事。兄文仲由校书郎迁礼部员外郎。<br /></div>
-----end

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　任宣州知州。与平仲有诗唱和。作品：之官宣城赠毅父次其韵。除宣城守赠元忠毅父次其韵。<div id='poem_58075' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58075' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58075?labeling=true' target='_blank'>之官宣城赠毅父次其韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58075")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58075_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58075'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58075'>几夕林声酝造秋，移船回指凤凰楼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58075'>身疲禁内凝严地，恩与江南爽垲州。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58075'>历数近城多异境，问知前政尽名流。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58075'>嘉观胜赏应难尽，更为吟哦万古愁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58075'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58075_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58007' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58007' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58007")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_58007_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58007'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58007'>垂杨正好移舟看，轻舸何妨出沐迟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58007_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58007'>叠嶂双溪虽未历，白云芳草已相知。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58007_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58007'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_58007_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　任宣州知州。与吴子权有诗唱和。作品：宣州吴子权送陵阳酒。<div id='poem_58199' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58199' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58199?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宣州吴子权送陵阳酒</a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58199")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58199_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58199'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58199'>梦寐陵阳天上山，曾将心约白云閒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58199_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58199'>仙衔已下青冥里，尘骨难留缥缈间。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58199_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58199'>三尺溪鱼如可控，千年辽鹤尚应还。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58199_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58199'>多情别后能论旧，远寄官醪为解颜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58199_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58199'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58199_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　任宣州知州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　再除知宣州。弟平仲除知衡州，有诗送平仲。作品：送毅父弟知衡州。<div id='poem_58235' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58235' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58235?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送殷父弟知衡州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_58235")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58235_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58235'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58235'>浮云富贵本无情，出守衡阳地望清。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58235_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58235'>陇亩良田多乐岁，江山秀气入重城。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58235_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58235'>铃斋宴衎茶樽佚，棠荫优游狱讼平。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58235_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58235'>应念区区大梁客，朝衣颠倒趁鸡鸣<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《清江三孔集》卷七）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58235_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58235'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58235_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年1月11日</a>　任宣州知州。作记。作品：筠州无讼堂记。<div id='poem_1194181' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1194181' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1194181?labeling=true' target='_blank'>筠州无讼堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年1月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24355, "北宋", "孔武仲", "poem_title_1194181")'>孔武仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1194181_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1194181'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1194181'>筠州刺史治舍，前临蜀江，后接山谷，相传以为仙人李八百之所居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1194181_comment'></div>其地与市井绝，造舟为梁，以通往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1194181_comment'></div>故其门庭靓深，有洞府之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1194181_comment'></div>自厅事以北，林木相重，间以华屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1194181_comment'></div>有堂在中，名曰无讼堂，朝散郎许公长卿之所建也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1194181_comment'></div>筠，江西支郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1194181_comment'></div>始者，市区寂寥，人物鲜少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1194181_comment'></div>近岁乃更昌大蕃富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1194181_comment'></div>其属邑布在险阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1194181_comment'></div>乐岁，粒米狼戾，而四方商贾不能至，囷仓之积，守之至白首而不发，茍治之有方，足以无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1194181_comment'></div>许君之来，因其风俗，示以法度，以忠信简约行之期年，民大信服，狱讼稀少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1194181_comment'></div>暇日登斯堂，与宾客从容究民疾苦，求所以善其后者，则君之命堂，其意可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1194181_comment'></div>尝闻为吏者，其资不同，而功效亦异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1194181_comment'></div>处诚履素，以忠利惕隐为民宗主，人望其容貌，而争意销亡，此德之盛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1194181_comment'></div>先事立决，事至立断，直者伸矣，奸伪遁逃，此之谓敏决也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1194181_comment'></div>民怀其不平，出于山泽之中，裸粮百里以赴愬于上，夹以锐木，临以白梃，惷愚者望风股栗，逡巡而退，亦足为无讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1194181_comment'></div>复有畏惮大吏，以矜饰取容，寓狱于门，匿民于市，积月踰时，不为持省，而囹圄亦空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1194181_comment'></div>其形甚似，而离实远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1194181_comment'></div>许君，良吏也，吾可以无忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1194181_comment'></div>然亦不可不为方来者戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1194181_comment'></div>绍圣四年正月十一日，鲁国孔某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1194181_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
